                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.5"><label>ut.1.5</label> śālākyatantrābhihitā

                        <caesura/>
                         upasargādayo rogā ye cāpy āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.7"><label>ut.1.7</label> triṣaṣṭī rasasaṃsargāḥ svasthavṛttaṃ

                        <caesura/>
                         yuktārthā yuktayaś caiva doṣabhedās tathaiva ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.8"><label>ut.1.8</label> yatroktā vividhā arthā
                        rogasādhanahetavaḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.9"><label>ut.1.9</label> ādāv evottamāṅgasthān rogān
                        abhidadhāmy aham |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṅkhyayā lakṣaṇaiś cāpi sādhyāsādhyakrameṇa ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.10"><label>ut.1.10</label> vidyāddvayaṅgulabāhulyaṃ
                        svāṅguṣṭhodarasaṃmitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dvyaṅgulaṃ sarvataḥ sārdhaṃ bhiṣaṅnayanabudbudam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.11"><label>ut.1.11</label> suvṛttaṃ gostanākāraṃ
                        sarvabhūtaguṇodbhavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         palaṃ bhuvo 'gnito raktaṃ vātāt kṛṣṇaṃ sitaṃ jalāt || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.12"><label>ut.1.12</label> ākāśādaśrumārgāś ca jāyante
                        netrabudbude |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭiṃ cātra tathā vakṣye yathā brūyād viśāradaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.13"><label>ut.1.13</label> netrāyāmatribhāgaṃ tu
                        kṛṣṇamaṇḍalamucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇāt saptamam icchanti dṛṣṭiṃ dṛṣṭiviśāradāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.14"><label>ut.1.14</label> maṇḍalāni ca sandhīṃś ca paṭalāni
                        ca locane |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathākramaṃ vijānīyāt pañca ṣaṭ ca ṣaḍeva ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.15"><label>ut.1.15</label> pakṣmavartmaśvetakṛṣṇadṛṣṭīnāṃ
                        maṇḍalāni tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         anupūrvaṃ tu te madhyāś catvāro 'ntyā yathottaram || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.16"><label>ut.1.16</label> pakṣmavartmagataḥ
                        sandhirvartmaśuklagato 'paraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklakṛṣṇagatastvanyaḥ kṛṣṇadṛṣṭigato 'paraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kanīnakagataḥ ṣaṣṭhaś cāpāṅgagaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.17"><label>ut.1.17</label> dve vartmapaṭale vidyāc
                        catvāryanyāni cākṣiṇi |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāyate timiraṃ yeṣu vyādhiḥ paramadāruṇaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.18"><label>ut.1.18</label> tejojalāśritaṃ bāhyaṃ teṣv anyat
                        piśitāśritam |
                        <caesura/>
                         medastṛtīyaṃ paṭalamāśritaṃ tvasthi cāparam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.19"><label>ut.1.19</label> pañcamāṃśasamaṃ dṛṣṭesteṣāṃ
                        bāhulpamiṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         sirāṇāṃ kaṇḍarāṇāṃ ca medasaḥ kālakasya ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.20"><label>ut.1.20</label> guṇāḥ kālāt paraḥ śleṣmā bandhane
                        'kṣṇoḥ sirāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sirānusāribhir doṣair viguṇair ūrdhvamāgataiḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.21"><label>ut.1.21</label> jāyante netrabhāgeṣu rogāḥ
                        paramadāruṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāvilaṃ sasaṃrambhamaśrukaṇḍūpadehavat<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.22"><label>ut.1.22</label> gurūṣātodarāgādyairjuṣṭaṃ
                        cāvyaktalakṣaṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśūlaṃ vartmakoṣeṣu śūkapūrṇābham eva ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.23"><label>ut.1.23</label> vihanyamānaṃ rūpe vā kriyāsvakṣi
                        yathā purā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭvaiva dhīmān budhyeta doṣeṇādhiṣṭhitaṃ tu tat || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.24"><label>ut.1.24</label> tatra saṃbhavamāsādya yathādoṣaṃ
                        bhiṣagjitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidadhyānnetrajā rogā balavantaḥ syuranyathā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.25"><label>ut.1.25</label> saṅkṣepataḥ kriyāyogo
                        nidānaparivarjanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātādīnāṃ pratīghātaḥ prokto vistarataḥ punaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.26"><label>ut.1.26</label> uṣṇābhitaptasya
                        jalapraveśāddūrekṣaṇāt svapnaviparyayāc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasaktasaṃrodanakopaśokakleśābhighātādatimaithunāc ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.27"><label>ut.1.27</label>
                        śuktāranālāmlakulatthamāṣaniṣevaṇādvegavinigrahāc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedādatho dhūmaniṣevaṇāc ca chardervighātādvamanātiyogāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         bāṣpagrahāt sūkṣmanirīkṣaṇāc ca netre vikārān janayanti doṣāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.28"><label>ut.1.28</label> vātāddaśa tathā pittāt kaphāc caiva
                        trayodaśa |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktāt ṣoḍaśa vijñeyāḥ sarvajāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.29"><label>ut.1.29</label> tathā bāhyau punardvau ca rogāḥ
                        ṣaṭsaptatiḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hatādhimantho nimiṣo dṛṣṭirgambhīrikā ca yā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.30"><label>ut.1.30</label> yac ca vātahataṃ vartma na te
                        sidhyanti vātajāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yāpyo 'tha tanmayaḥ kācaḥ sādhyāḥ syuḥsānyamārutāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.31"><label>ut.1.31</label>
                        śuṣkākṣipākādhīmanthasyandamārutapryayāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyo hrasvajāḍyo yo jalasrāvaś ca paittikaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.32"><label>ut.1.32</label> parimlāyī ca nīlaś ca yāpyaḥ kāco
                        'tha tanmayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhiṣyando 'dhimantho 'mlādhyuṣitaṃ śuktikā ca yā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.33"><label>ut.1.33</label> dṛṣṭiḥ pittavidagdhā ca dhūmadarśī
                        ca sidhyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyaḥ kaphajaḥ srāvo yāpyaḥ kācaś ca tanmayaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.34"><label>ut.1.34</label> abhiṣyando 'dhimanthaś ca
                        balāsagrathitaṃ ca yat |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭiḥ śleṣmavidagdhā ca pothakyo lagaṇaś ca yaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.35"><label>ut.1.35</label><ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker"
                        >1</ref>krimigranthipariklinnavartmaśuklārmapiṣṭakāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmopanāhaḥ sādhyās tu kathitāḥ śleṣmajeṣu tu || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.36"><label>ut.1.36</label> raktasrāvo 'jakājātaṃ
                        śoṇitārśovraṇānvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śukraṃ na sādhyaṃ kācaś ca yāpyastajjaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.37"><label>ut.1.37</label> manthasyandau <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote        marker">1</ref>kliṣṭavartma
                        harṣotpātau tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sirājātāñjanākhyā ca sirājālaṃ ca yat smṛtam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.38"><label>ut.1.38</label> parvaṇyathāvraṇaṃ śukraṃ
                        śoṇitārmārjunaś ca yaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete sādhyā vikāreṣu raktajeṣu bhavanti hi || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.39"><label>ut.1.39</label> pūyāsrāvo nākulāndhyamakṣipākātyayo
                        'lajī |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyāḥ sarvajā yāpyaḥ kācaḥ kopaś ca pakṣmaṇaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.40"><label>ut.1.40</label> vartmāvabandho yo vyādhiḥ sirāsu
                        piḍakā ca yā |
                        <caesura/>
                         prastāryarmādhimāṃsārma snāyvarmotsaṅginī ca yā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.41"><label>ut.1.41</label> pūyālasaś cārbudaṃ ca
                        śyāvakardamavartmanī |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathārśovartma śuṣkārśaḥ śarkarāvartma yac ca vai || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.42"><label>ut.1.42</label> saśophaś cāpy aśophaś ca pāko
                        bahalavartma ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         aklinnavartma kumbhīkā bisavartma ca sidhyati || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.43"><label>ut.1.43</label> sanimitto 'nimittaś ca dvāv
                        asādhyau tu bāhyajau |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṭsaptatir vikārāṇām eṣā saṃgrahakīrtitā<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.44"><label>ut.1.44</label> nava sandhyāśrayās teṣu vartmajās
                        tv ekaviṃśatiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklabhāge daśaikaś ca catvāraḥ kṛṣṇabhāgajāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.1.45"><label>ut.1.45</label> sarvāśrayāḥ saptadaśa dṛṣṭijā
                        dvādaśaiva tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         bāhyajau dvau samākhyātau rogau paramadāruṇau |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūya etān pravakṣyāmi saṅkhyārūpacikitsitaiḥ ||</l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre

                <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.1"><label>ut.2.1</label> athātaḥ sandhigatarogavijñānīyam
                        adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.2"><label>ut.2.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.3a"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.4a"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.5a"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.6a"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.3"><label>ut.2.3</label> pūyālasaḥ sopanāhaḥ srāvāḥ
                        parvaṇikālajī |
                        <caesura/>
                         krimigranthiś ca vijñeyā rogāḥ sandhigatā nava || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.4"><label>ut.2.4</label> pakvaḥ śophaḥ sandhijaḥ saṃsravedyaḥ
                        sāndraṃ pūyaṃ pūti pūyālasaḥ saḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         granthirnālpo dṛṣṭisandhāvapākaḥ kaṇḍūprāyo nīrujastūpanāhaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.5"><label>ut.2.5</label> gatvā sandhīnaśrumārgeṇa doṣāḥ kuryuḥ
                        srāvān rugvihīnān kanīnāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         tān vai srāvān netranāḍīm athaike tasyā liṅgaṃ kīrtayiṣye caturdhā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.6"><label>ut.2.6</label> pākaḥ sandhau saṃsravedyaś ca pūyaṃ
                        pūyāsrāvo naikarūpaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvetaṃ sāndraṃ picchilaṃ saṃsravedyaḥ śleṣmāsrāvo nīrujaḥ sa pradiṣṭaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.7"><label>ut.2.7</label> raktāsrāvaḥ śoṇitotthaḥ saraktamuṣṇaṃ
                        nālpaṃ saṃsravennātisāndram |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītābhāsaṃ nīlamuṣṇaṃ jalābhaṃ pittāsrāvaḥ saṃsravet sandhimadhyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.8"><label>ut.2.8</label> tāmrā tanvī dāhaśūlopapannā
                        raktājjñeyā parvaṇī vṛttaśophā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jātā sandhau kṛṣṇaśukle 'lajī syāt tasminn eva khyāpitā pūrvaliṅgaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.2.9"><label>ut.2.9</label> krimigranthirvartmanaḥ pakṣmaṇaś ca
                        kaṇḍūṃ kuryuḥ krimayaḥ sandhijātāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nānārūpā vartmaśuklasya sandhau caranto 'ntarnayanaṃ dūṣayanti ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre sandhigatarogavijñānīyo nāma
                        dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||2 ||</p>
                </div>



                <div n="3" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.1"><label>ut.3.1</label> athāto
                        vartmagatarogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.2"><label>ut.3.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.3"><label>ut.3.3</label> pṛthagdoṣāḥ samastā vā yadā
                        vartmavyapāśrayāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sirā vyāpyāvatiṣṭhante vartmasvadhikamūrcchitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.4"><label>ut.3.4</label> vivardhya māṃsaṃ raktaṃ ca tadā
                        vartmavyapāśrayān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikārāñjanayanty āśu nāmatas tān nibodhata || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.5"><label>ut.3.5</label> utsaṅginyatha kumbhīkā pothakyo
                        vartmaśarkarā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathārśovartma śuṣkārśastathaivāñjananāmikā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.6"><label>ut.3.6</label> bahalaṃ vartma yaccāpi
                        vyādhirvartmāvabandhakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kliṣṭakardamavartmākhyau śyāvavartma tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.7"><label>ut.3.7</label> praklinnamapariklinnaṃ vartma
                        vātahataṃ tu yat |
                        <caesura/>
                         arbudaṃ nimiṣaś cāpi śoṇitārśaś ca yat smṛtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.8"><label>ut.3.8</label> lagaṇo biśanāmā ca pakṣmakopas
                        tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaviṃśatirityete vikārā vartmasaṃśrayāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.9"><label>ut.3.9</label> nāmabhis te samuddiṣṭā lakṣaṇaistān
                        pracakṣmahe |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhyantaramukhī bāhyotsaṅge 'dho vartmanaś ca<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> yā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.10"><label>ut.3.10</label> vijñeyotsaṅginī nāma
                        tadrūpapiḍakācitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kumbhīkabījapratimāḥ piḍakā <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>yās tu vartmajāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.11"><label>ut.3.11</label> ādhmāpayanti bhinnā yāḥ
                        kumbhīkapiḍakās tu tāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         srāviṇyaḥ kaṇḍurā gurvyo raktasarṣapasannibhāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         piḍakāś ca rujāvatyaḥ pothakya iti saṃjñitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.12"><label>ut.3.12</label> piḍakābhiḥ susūkṣmābhir ghanābhir
                        abhisaṃvṛtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         piḍakā yā kharā sthūlā sā jñeyā vartmaśarkarā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.13"><label>ut.3.13</label> ervārubījapratimāḥ piḍakā
                        mandavedanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sūkṣmāḥ kharāś ca vartmasthāstadarśovartma kīrtyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.14"><label>ut.3.14</label> dīrgho 'ṅkuraḥ kharaḥ stabdho
                        dāruṇo vartmasaṃbhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhireṣa samākhyātaḥ śuṣkārśa iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.15"><label>ut.3.15</label> dāhatodavatī tāmrā piḍakā
                        vartmasaṃbhavā |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdvī mandarujā sūkṣmā jñeyā sāñjananāmikā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.16"><label>ut.3.16</label> vartmopacīyate yasya piḍakābhiḥ
                        samantataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         savarṇābhiḥ samābhiś ca vidyādbahalavartma tat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.17"><label>ut.3.17</label> kaṇḍūmatālpatodena vartmaśophena yo
                        naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na samaṃ chādayed akṣi bhavedbandhaḥ sa vartmanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.18"><label>ut.3.18</label> mṛdvalpavedanaṃ tāmraṃ yadvartma
                        samam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         akasmāc ca bhaved raktaṃ kliṣṭavartma tad ādiśet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.19"><label>ut.3.19</label> kliṣṭaṃ punaḥ pittayutaṃ vidahec
                        choṇitaṃ yadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā klinnatvam āpannam ucyate vartmakardamaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.20"><label>ut.3.20</label> yad vartma bāhyato 'nyaś ca śyāvaṃ
                        śūnaṃ savedanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhakaṇḍūparikledi śyāvavartmeti tan matam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.21"><label>ut.3.21</label> arujaṃ bāhyataḥ śūnamantaḥ klinnaṃ
                        sravaty api |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṇḍūnis todabhūyiṣṭhaṃ klinnavartma tad ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.22"><label>ut.3.22</label> yasya dhautāni dhautāni
                        saṃbadhyante punaḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vartmānyaparipakvāni vidyādaklinnavartma tat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.23"><label>ut.3.23</label> vimuktasandhi niś ceṣṭaṃ vartma
                        yasya na mīlyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         etadvātahataṃ vidyāt sarujaṃ yadi vārujam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.24"><label>ut.3.24</label> vartmāntarasthaṃ viṣamaṃ
                        granthibhūtamavedanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vijñeyamarbudaṃ puṃsāṃ saraktamavalambitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.25"><label>ut.3.25</label> nimeṣaṇīḥ sirā vāyuḥ praviṣṭo
                        vartmasaṃśrayāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cālayatyati vartmāni nimeṣaḥ sa gado mataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.26"><label>ut.3.26</label> chinnāś chinā vivardhante
                        vartmasthā mṛdavo 'ṅkurāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhakaṇḍūrujopetāste 'rśaḥ śoṇitasaṃbhavāḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.27"><label>ut.3.27</label> apākaḥ kaṭhinaḥ sthūlo
                        granthirvartmabhavo 'rujaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakaṇḍūḥ picchilaḥ kolapramāṇo lagaṇas tu saḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.28"><label>ut.3.28</label> śūnaṃ yadvartma bahubhiḥ sūkṣmaiś
                        chidraiḥ samanvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         bisamantarjala iva bisavartmeti tanmatam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.29"><label>ut.3.29</label> doṣāḥ pakṣmāśayagatāstīkṣṇāgrāṇi
                        kharāṇi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirvartayanti pakṣmāṇi tairghuṣṭaṃ cākṣi dūyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.3.30"><label>ut.3.30</label> uddhṛtair uddhṛtaiḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> śāntiḥ pakṣmabhiś copajāyate
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātātapānaladveṣī pakṣmakopaḥ sa ucyate ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre vartmagatarogavijñānīyo nāma
                        tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||3 ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="4" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.1"><label>ut.4.1</label> athātaḥ śuklagatarogavijñānīyam
                        adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.2"><label>ut.4.2</label> athovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.3"><label>ut.4.3</label>
                        prastāriśuklakṣatajādhimāṃsasrāyvarmasaṃjñāḥ khalu pañcarogāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         syuḥ śuktikā cārjunapiṣṭakau ca jālaṃ sirāṇāṃ piḍakāś ca yāḥ syuḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.4"><label>ut.4.4</label> rogā balāsagrathitena sārdham
                        ekādaśākṣṇoḥ khalu śuklabhāge |
                        <caesura/>
                         prastāri prathitam ihārma śuklabhāge vistīrṇaṃ tanu rudhiraprabhaṃ sanīlam
                        || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.5"><label>ut.4.5</label> śuklākhyaṃ mṛdu kathayanti śuklabhāge
                        saśvetaṃ samam iha vardhate cireṇa |
                        <caesura/>
                         yan māṃsaṃ pracayam upaiti śuklabhāge padmābhaṃ tad upadiśanti lohitārma || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.6"><label>ut.4.6</label> vistīrṇaṃ mṛdu bahalaṃ yakṛtprakāśaṃ
                        śyāvaṃ vā tad adhikamāṃsajārma vidyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         śukle yat piśitam upaiti vṛddhim etat snāyvarmety abhipaṭhitaṃ kharaṃ
                        prapāṇḍu || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.7"><label>ut.4.7</label> śyāvāḥ syuḥ piśitanibhāś ca bindavo
                        ye śuktyābhāḥ sitanayane sa śuktisaṃjñaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         eko yaḥ śaśarudhiropamas tu binduḥ śuklastho bhavati tam arjunaṃ vadanti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.8"><label>ut.4.8</label> utsannaḥ salilanibho 'tha piṣṭaśuklo
                        bindur yo bhavati sa piṣṭakaḥ suvṛttaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jālābhaḥ kaṭhinasiro mahān saraktaḥ santānaḥ smṛta iha jālasaṃjñitas tu || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.4.9"><label>ut.4.9</label> śuklasthāḥ sitapiḍakāḥ sirāvṛtā yās
                        tā vidyād asitasamīpajāḥ sirājāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāṃsyābho bhavati site 'mbubindutulyaḥ sa jñeyo 'mṛdurarujo balāsakākhyaḥ
                        ||</l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre śuklagatarogavijñānīyo nāma
                        caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ ||4 ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="5" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.1"><label>ut.5.1</label> athātaḥ
                        kṛṣṇagatarogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.2"><label>ut.5.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.3"><label>ut.5.3</label> yat savraṇaṃ śukla(śukra)mathāvraṇaṃ
                        vā pākātyayaś cāpy ajakā tathaiva |
                        <caesura/>
                         catvāra ete 'bhihitā vikārāḥ kṛṣṇāśrayāḥ saṃgrahataḥ purastāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.4"><label>ut.5.4</label> nimagnarūpaṃ hi bhavet tu kṛṣṇe
                        sūcyeva viddhaṃ pratibhāti <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>yadvai |
                        <caesura/>
                         srāvaṃ sraveduṣṇamatīva ruk ca tat savraṇaṃ śukra(śukla)mudāharanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.5"><label>ut.5.5</label> dṛṣṭeḥ samīpe na bhavet tu yac ca na
                        cāvagāḍhaṃ na ca saṃsraveddhi |
                        <caesura/>
                         avedanāvan na ca yugmaśukraṃ tatsiddhimāpnoti kadācideva || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.6"><label>ut.5.6</label> vicchinnamadhyaṃ piśitāvṛtaṃ vā calaṃ
                        sirāsaktamadṛṣṭikṛc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dvitvaggataṃ lohitamantataś ca cirotthitaṃ cāpi vivarjanīyam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.7"><label>ut.5.7</label> uṣṇāśrupātaḥ piḍakā ca kṛṣṇe yasmin
                        bhaven mudganibhaṃ ca śukram |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad apy asādhyaṃ pravadanti kecidanyac ca yat tittiripakṣatulyam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.8ab"><label>ut.5.8</label> sitaṃ yadā bhāty asitapradeśe
                        syandātmakaṃ nātirugaśruyuktam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.8cd"> vihāyasīvāc chaghanānukāri<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> tad avraṇaṃ sādhyatamaṃ
                        vadanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.9"><label>ut.5.9</label> gambhīrajātaṃ bahalaṃ ca śukraṃ
                        cirotthitaṃ cāpi vadanti kṛcchram |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃcchādyate śvetanibhena sarvaṃ doṣeṇa yasyāsitamaṇḍalaṃ tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.5.10"><label>ut.5.10</label>
                            tamakṣipākātyayamakṣikopasamutthitaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> tīvrarujaṃ vadanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajāpurīṣapratimo rujāvān salohito lohitapicchilāśruḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārya kṛṣṇaṃ pracayo 'bhyupaiti taṃ cājakājātam iti vyavasyet ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre kṛṣṇagatarogavijñānīyo nāma
                        pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||5 ||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="6" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.1"><label>ut.6.1</label> athātaḥ
                        sarvagatarogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.2"><label>ut.6.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.3"><label>ut.6.3</label> syandās tu catvāra ihopadiṣṭāstāvanta
                        eveha tathādhimanthāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophānvito 'śophayutaś ca pākāv ity evam ete daśa saṃpradiṣṭāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.4"><label>ut.6.4</label> hatādhimantho 'nilaparyayaś ca
                        śuṣkākṣipāko 'nyata eva vātaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭistatathāmlādhyuṣitā sirāṇāmutpātaharṣāvapi sarvabhāgāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.5"><label>ut.6.5</label> prāyeṇa sarve nayanāmayāstu
                        bhavantyabhiṣyandanimittamūlāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād abhiṣyandamudīryamāṇamupācaredāśu hitāya dhīmān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.6"><label>ut.6.6</label> nistodanaṃ
                        stambhanaromaharṣasaṅgharṣapāruṣyaśirobhitāpāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśuṣkabhāvaḥ śiśirāśrutā ca vātābhipanne nayane bhavanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.7"><label>ut.6.7</label> dāhaprapākau śiśirābhinandā
                        dhūmāyanaṃ bāṣpasamucchrayaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇāśrutā pītakanetratā ca pittābhipanne nayane bhavanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.8"><label>ut.6.8</label> uṣṇābhinandā gurutākṣiśophaḥ
                        kaṇḍūpadehau sitatātiśaityam |
                        <caesura/>
                         srāvo muhuḥ picchila eva cāpi kaphābhipanne nayane bhavanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.9"><label>ut.6.9</label> tāmrāśrutā lohitanetratā ca rājyaḥ
                        samantādatilohitāś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittasya liṅgāni ca yāni tāni raktābhipanne nayane bhavanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.10"><label>ut.6.10</label>
                        vṛddhairetairabhiṣyandairnarāṇāmakriyāvatām |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāvantastvadhimanthāḥ syurnayane tīvravedanāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.11"><label>ut.6.11</label> utpāṭyata ivātyarthaṃ netraṃ
                        nirmathyate tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śiraso 'rdhaṃ ca taṃ vidyādadhimanthaṃ svalakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.12"><label>ut.6.12</label> netramutpāṭyata iva mathyate
                        'raṇivac ca yat |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṅgharṣatodanirbhedamāṃsasaṃrabdhamāvilam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.13"><label>ut.6.13</label>
                        kuñcanāsphoṭanādhmānavepathuvyathanairyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śiraso 'rdhaṃ ca yena syādadhimanthaḥ sa mārutāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.14"><label>ut.6.14</label> raktarājicitaṃ srāvi
                        vahninevāvadahyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         yakṛtpiṇḍopamaṃ dāhi kṣāreṇāktamiva kṣatam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.15"><label>ut.6.15</label> prapakvocchūnavartmāntaṃ sasvedaṃ
                        pītadarśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāśirodāhayutaṃ pittenākṣyadhimanthitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.16"><label>ut.6.16</label> śophavannātisaṃrabdhaṃ
                        srāvakaṇḍūsamanvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śaityagauravapaicchilyadūṣikāharṣaṇānvitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.17"><label>ut.6.17</label> rūpaṃ paśyati duḥkhena
                        pāṃśupūrṇamivāvilam |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsādhmānaśiroduḥkhayutaṃ śleṣmādhimanthitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.18"><label>ut.6.18</label> bandhujīvapratīkāśaṃ tāmyati
                        sparśanākṣamam |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktāsrāvaṃ sanistodaṃ paśyaty agninibhā diśaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.19"><label>ut.6.19</label> raktāmagnāriṣṭavac ca kṛṣṇabhāgaś
                        ca lakṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         yad dīptaṃ raktaparyantaṃ tad raktenādhimanthitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.20"><label>ut.6.20</label> hanyādṛṣṭiṃ saptarātrāt kaphottho
                        'dhīmantho 'sṛksaṃbhavaḥ pañcarātrāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaḍrātrādvau mārutottho nihanyān mithyācārāt paittikaḥ sadya eva || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.21ab"><label>ut.6.21</label> kaṇḍūpadehāśruyutaḥ
                        pakvodumbarasannibhaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.21cd"> dāhasaṃharṣatāmratvaśophanistodagauravaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.22ab"><label>ut.6.22</label> juṣṭo muhuḥ sravec cāsram
                        uṣṇaśītāmbu picchilam | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.22cd"> saṃrambhī pacyate yaś ca netrapākaḥ saśophajaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.23"><label>ut.6.23</label> śophahīnāni liṅgāni netrapāke tv
                        aśophaje |
                        <caesura/>
                         upekṣaṇādakṣi yadādhimantho vātātmakaḥ sādayati prasahya |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujābhir ugrābhir asādhya eṣa hatādhimanthaḥ khalu nāma rogaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.24"><label>ut.6.24</label> antaḥsirāṇāṃ śvasanaḥ sthito dṛṣṭiṃ
                        pratikṣipan |
                        <caesura/>
                         hatādhimanthaṃ janayet tam asādhyaṃ vidur budhāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.25"><label>ut.6.25</label> pakṣmadvayākṣibhruvamāśritastu
                        yannānilaḥ saṃcarati praduṣṭaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paryāyaśaś cāpi rujaḥ karoti taṃ vātaparyāyamudāharanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.26"><label>ut.6.26</label> yat kūṇitaṃ dāruṇarūkṣavartma
                        vilokane cāviladarśanaṃ yat |
                        <caesura/>
                         sudāruṇaṃ yat pratibodhane ca śuṣkākṣipākopahataṃ tadakṣi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.27"><label>ut.6.27</label> yasyāvaṭūkarṇaśirohanustho
                        manyāgato vāpyanilo 'nyato vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryād rujo 'ti bhruvi locane vā tamanyatovātamudāharanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.28"><label>ut.6.28</label> amlena bhuktena vidāhinā ca
                        saṃchādyate sarvata eva netram |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophānvitaṃ lohitakaiḥ sanīlairetādṛgamlādhyuṣitaṃ vadanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.29"><label>ut.6.29</label> avedanā vāpi savedanā vā
                        yasyākṣirājyo hi bhavanti tāmrāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         muhurvirajyanti ca tāḥ samantād vyādhiḥ sirotpāta iti pradiṣṭaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.6.30"><label>ut.6.30</label> mohāt sirotpāta upekṣitas tu jāyeta
                        rogas tu sirāpraharṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāmrācchamasraṃ sravati pragāḍhaṃ tathā na śaknotyabhivīkṣituṃ ca ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre sarvagatarogavijñānīyo nāma
                        ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ ||6 ||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="7" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.1"><label>ut.7.1</label> athāto

                         śītasātmyāṃ nṛṇāṃ dṛṣṭimāhurnayanacintakāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.5"><label>ut.7.5</label> rogāṃstadāśrayān ghorān ṣaṭ ca ṣaṭ ca

                         paṭalānupraviṣṭasya timirasya ca lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.7"><label>ut.7.7</label> avyaktāni sa rūpāṇi sarvāṇyeva

                        <caesura/>
                         tathā naraḥ pittavidagdhadṛṣṭiḥ kaphena cānyastvatha dhūmadarśī || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.35"><label>ut.7.35</label> yo hrasvajāḍyo<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>(hrasvajātyo) nakulāndhatā ca
                        gambhīrasaṃjñā ca tathaiva dṛṣṭiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittena duṣṭena gatena dṛṣṭiṃ pītā bhavedyasya narasya dṛṣṭiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.36"><label>ut.7.36</label> pītāni rūpāṇi ca manyate yaḥ sa
                        mānavaḥ pittavidagdhadṛṣṭiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāpte tṛtīyaṃ paṭalaṃ tu doṣe divā na paśyenniśi vīkṣate ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.37"><label>ut.7.37</label> (<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref>rātrau sa śītānugṛhītadṛṣṭiḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.38"><label>ut.7.38</label> triṣu sthitolpaḥ paṭaleṣu doṣo

                        <caesura/>

                        >1</ref>sūryānugṛhītacakṣurīkṣeta rūpāṇi kaphālpabhāvāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.39"><label>ut.7.39</label> śokajvarāyāsaśirobhitāpairabhyāhatā
                        yasya narasya dṛṣṭiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadhūmakān paśyati sarvabhāvāṃstaṃ dhūmadarśīti vadanti rogam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.40"><label>ut.7.40</label> sa <ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref>hrasvajāḍyo divaseṣu

                        <caesura/>
                         vidyotate yena narasya dṛṣṭirdoṣābhipannā nakulasya yadvat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.41"><label>ut.7.41</label> citrāṇi rūpāṇi divā sa paśyet sa
                        vai vikāro nakulāndhyasaṃjñaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭirvirūpā śvasanopasṛṣṭā saṅkucyate 'bhyantarataś ca yāti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.42"><label>ut.7.42</label> rujāvagāḍhā ca tamakṣirogaṃ
                        gambhīriketi pravadanti tajjñāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bāhyau punardvāviha saṃpradiṣṭau nimittataś cāpy animittataś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.43"><label>ut.7.43</label> nimittatas tatra
                        śirobhitāpājjñeyastvabhiṣyandanidarśanaiś ca<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         surarṣigandharvamahoragāṇāṃ sandarśanenāpi ca bhāsvarāṇām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.44"><label>ut.7.44</label> hanyeta dṛṣṭirmanujasya yasya sa
                        liṅganāśastvanimittasaṃjñaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrākṣi vispaṣṭamivāvabhāti vaidūryavarṇā vimalā ca dṛṣṭiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.45"><label>ut.7.45</label> vidīryate sīdati hīyate vā
                        nṛṇāmabhīghātahatā tu dṛṣṭiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.7.46"><label>ut.7.46</label> ityete nayanagatā mayā vikārāḥ
                        saṃkhyātāḥ pṛthagiha ṣaṭ ca saptatiś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         eteṣāṃ pṛthagiha vistareṇa sarvaṃ vakṣye 'haṃ tadanu cikitsitaṃ yathāvat
                        ||</l>

                <div n="8" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.1"><label>ut.8.1</label> athātaś
                        cikitsitapravibhāgavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.2"><label>ut.8.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        (suśrutāya) ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.3"><label>ut.8.3</label> ṣaṭsaptatirye 'bhihitā vyādhayo
                        nāmalakṣaṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsitamidaṃ teṣāṃ samāsavyāsataḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> śṛṇu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.4"><label>ut.8.4</label> chedyāsteṣu daśaikaś ca nava lekhyāḥ
                        prakīrtitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhedyāḥ pañca vikārāḥ syurvyadhyāḥ pañcadaśaiva tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.5"><label>ut.8.5</label> dvādaśāśastrakṛtyāś ca yāpyāḥ sapta
                        bhavanti hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogā varjayitavyāḥ syurdaśa pañca ca jānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyau vā bhavetāṃ tu yāpyau cāgantusaṃjñitau || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.6"><label>ut.8.6</label> arśo 'nvitaṃ bhavati vartma tu
                        yattathārśaḥ śuṣkaṃ tathārbudamatho piḍakāḥ sirājāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jālaṃ sirājam api pañcavidhaṃ tathārma chedyā bhavanti saha parvaṇikāmayena
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.7"><label>ut.8.7</label> utsaṅginī bahalakardamavartmanī ca
                        śyāvaṃ ca yac ca paṭhitaṃ tviha baddhavartma |
                        <caesura/>
                         kliṣṭaṃ ca pothakiyutaṃ khalu yac ca vartma kumbhīkinī ca saha śarkarayā ca
                        lekhyāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.8"><label>ut.8.8</label> śleṣmopanāhalagaṇau ca bisaṃ ca
                        bhedyā granthiś ca yaḥ kṛmikṛto 'ñjananāmikā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ādau sirā nigaditās tu yayoḥ prayoge pākau ca yau nayanayoḥ pavano 'nyataś
                        ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.9"><label>ut.8.9</label> pūyālasānilaviparyayamanthasaṃjñāḥ
                        syandās tu yantyupaśamaṃ hi sirāvyadhena |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuṣkākṣipākakaphapittavidagdhadṛṣṭiṣvamlākhyaśukrasahitārjunapiṣṭakeṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.10"><label>ut.8.10</label>
                        aklinnavartmahutabhugdhvajadarśiśuktipraklinnavartmasu tathaiva balāsasaṃjñe
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         āgantunāmayayugena ca dūṣitāyāṃ dṛṣṭau na śastrapatanaṃ pravadanti tajjñāḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.8.11"><label>ut.8.11</label> saṃpaśyataḥ ṣaḍapi ye 'bhihitāstu
                        kācāste pakṣmakopasahitās tu bhavanti yāpyāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         catvāra eva pavanaprabhavāstvasādhyā dvau pittajau kaphanimittaja eka eva |
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭārdhakā rudhirajāś ca gadāstridoṣāstāvanta eva gaditāvapi bāhyajau dvau
                        ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        cikitsitapravibhāgavijñānīyo nāmāṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||8 ||</p>

                <div n="9" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>navamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.1"><label>ut.9.1</label> athāto vātābhiṣyandapratiṣedhaṃ

                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.3"><label>ut.9.3</label> purāṇasarpiṣā snigdhau

                         svedayitvā yathānyāyaṃ sirāmokṣeṇa yojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.4"><label>ut.9.4</label> saṃpādayed bastibhis tu samyak
                        snehavirecitau |
                        <caesura/>
                         tarpaṇaiḥ puṭapākaiś ca dhūmairāś cyotanais tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.5"><label>ut.9.5</label> nasyasnehaparīṣekaiḥ śirobastibhir
                        eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātaghnanūpajalajamāṃsāmlakvāthasecanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.6"><label>ut.9.6</label> snehaiś caturbhir uṣṇaiś ca
                        tatpītāmbaradhāraṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         payobhir vesavāraiś ca sālvaṇaiḥ pāyasais tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.7"><label>ut.9.7</label> bhiṣak saṃpādayed etāvupanāhaiś ca
                        pūjitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         grāmyānūpaudakarasaiḥ snigdhaiḥ phalarasānvitaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.8"><label>ut.9.8</label> susaṃskṛtaiḥ payobhiś ca tayor āhāra
                        iṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā copari bhaktasya sarpiḥpānaṃ(pāne) praśasyate<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.9"><label>ut.9.9</label> triphalākvāthasaṃsiddhaṃ kevalaṃ
                        jīrṇam eva vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ vātaharaiḥ kṣīraṃ prathamena gaṇena vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.10"><label>ut.9.10</label> snehāstailādvinā siddhā vātaghnais
                        tarpaṇe hitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snaihikaḥ puṭapākaś ca dhūmo nasyaṃ ca tadvidham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.11"><label>ut.9.11</label> nasyādiṣu sthirākṣīramadhurais
                        tailamiṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         eraṇḍapallave mūle tvaci vājaṃ payaḥ śṛtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.12"><label>ut.9.12</label> kaṇṭakāryāś ca mūleṣu sukhoṣṇaṃ
                        secane hitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavodīcyayaṣṭyāhvapippalībhiḥ śṛtaṃ payaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.13"><label>ut.9.13</label> hitamardhodakaṃ seke tathāś
                        cyotanam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         hrīberavakramañjiṣṭhodumbaratvakṣu sādhitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.14"><label>ut.9.14</label> sāmbhaś chāgaṃ payo vāpi śūlāś
                        cyotanam uttamam |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhukaṃ rajanīṃ pathyāṃ devadāruṃ ca peṣayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.15"><label>ut.9.15</label> ājena payasā śreṣṭhamabhiṣyande
                        tadañjanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         gairikaṃ saindhavaṃ kṛṣṇāṃ nāgaraṃ ca yathottaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.16"><label>ut.9.16</label> dviguṇaṃ piṣṭamadbhis tu
                        guṭikāñjanamiṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehāñjanaṃ hitaṃ cātra vakṣyate tadyathāvidhi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.17"><label>ut.9.17</label> rogo yaś cānyatovāto yaś ca
                        mārutaparyayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anenaiva vidhānena bhiṣak tāvapi sādhayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.18"><label>ut.9.18</label> pūrvabhaktaṃ hitaṃ sarpiḥ kṣīraṃ
                        vāpyatha bhojane |
                        <caesura/>
                         vṛkṣādanyāṃ kapitthe ca pañcamūle mahatyapi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.19"><label>ut.9.19</label> sakṣīraṃ karkaṭarase siddhaṃ cātra
                        ghṛtaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ vā hitamatrāhuḥ pattūrārtagalāgnikaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.20"><label>ut.9.20</label> sakṣīraṃ meṣaśṛṅgyā vā
                        sarpirvīratareṇa vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavaṃ dāru śuṇṭhī ca mātuluṅgaraso ghṛtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.21"><label>ut.9.21</label> stanyodakābhyāṃ kartavyaṃ śuṣkapāke
                        tadañjanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūjitaṃ sarpiṣaś cātra pānamakṣṇoś ca tarpaṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.22"><label>ut.9.22</label> ghṛtena jīvanīyena nasyaṃ tailena
                        cāṇunā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pariṣeke hitaṃ cātra payaḥ śītaṃ sasaindhavam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.23"><label>ut.9.23</label> rajanīdārusiddhaṃ vā saindhavena
                        samāyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiryutaṃ stanyaghṛṣṭam añjanaṃ vā mahauṣadham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.24"><label>ut.9.24</label> vasā vānūpajalajā saindhavena
                        samāyutā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāgaronmiśritā kiñcicchuṣkapāke tadañjanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.9.25"><label>ut.9.25</label> pavanaprabhavā rogā ye
                        keciddṛṣṭināśanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bījenānena matimān teṣu karma prayojayet ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        vātābhiṣyandapratiṣedho nāma navamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||9 ||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="10" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.1"><label>ut.10.1</label> athātaḥ pittābhiṣyandapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.2"><label>ut.10.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.3"><label>ut.10.3</label> pittasyande paittike cādhimanthe
                        raktāsrāvaḥ sraṃsanaṃ cāpi kāryam |
                        <caesura/>
                         akṣṇoḥ sekālepanasyāñjanāni paitte ca syādyadvisarpe vidhānam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.4"><label>ut.10.4</label> gundrāṃ śāliṃ śaivalaṃ śailabhedaṃ
                        dārvīmelāmutpalaṃ rodhramabhram |
                        <caesura/>
                         padmātpatraṃ śarkarā darbhamikṣuṃ tālaṃ rodhraṃ vetasaṃ padmakaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.5"><label>ut.10.5</label> drākṣāṃ kṣaudraṃ candanaṃ
                        yaṣṭikāhvaṃ yoṣitkṣīraṃ rātryanante ca piṣṭvā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥsiddhaṃ tarpaṇe sekanasye<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> śastaṃ kṣīraṃ siddhameteṣu cājam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.6"><label>ut.10.6</label> yojyo vargo vyasta eṣo 'nyathā vā
                        samyaṅnasye 'ṣṭārdhasaṃkhye 'pi nityam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāḥ sarvāḥ pittaharyaḥ praśastāstryahāccordhvaṃ kṣīrasarpiś ca <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>nasyam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.7"><label>ut.10.7</label> pālāśaṃ syācchoṇitaṃ cāñjanārthe
                        śallakyā vā śarkarākṣaudrayuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakriyāṃ śarkarākṣaudrayuktāṃ pālindyāṃ vā madhuke vāpi kuryāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.8"><label>ut.10.8</label> mustā phenaḥ sāgarasyotpalaṃ ca
                        kṛmighnailādhātribījādrasaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tālīśailāgairikośīraśaṅkhair eva ṃ yuñjyādañjanaṃ stanyapiṣṭaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.9"><label>ut.10.9</label> cūrṇaṃ kuryād añjanārthe raso vā
                        stanyopeto dhātakīsyandanābhyām |
                        <caesura/>
                         yoṣitstanyaṃ śātakumbhaṃ vighṛṣṭaṃ kṣaudropetaṃ kaiśukaṃ cāpi puṣpam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.10"><label>ut.10.10</label> rodhraṃ drākṣāṃ śarkarāmutpalaṃ
                        ca nāryāḥ kṣīre yaṣṭikāhvaṃ vacāṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭvā kṣīre varṇakasya tvacaṃ ca toyonmiśre candanodumbare ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.11"><label>ut.10.11</label> kāryaḥ phenaḥ sāgarasyāñjanārthe
                        nārīstanye mākṣike cāpi ghṛṣṭaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yoṣitstanye sthāpitaṃ yaṣṭikāhvaṃ rodhraṃ drākṣāṃ śarkarāmutpalaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.12"><label>ut.10.12</label> kṣaumābaddhaṃ pathyamāś cyotane
                        vā sarpirghṛṣṭaṃ yaṣṭikāhvaṃ sarodhram |
                        <caesura/>
                         toyonmiśrāḥ kāśmarīdhātripathyāstadvaccāhuḥ kaṭphalaṃ cāmbunaiva || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.13"><label>ut.10.13</label> eṣo 'mlākhye 'nukramaś cāpi
                        śuktau kāryaḥ sarvaḥ syātsirāmokṣavarjyaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.14"><label>ut.10.14</label> sarpiḥ peyaṃ traiphalaṃ tailvakaṃ
                        vā peyaṃ vā syāt kevalaṃ yat purāṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣe 'dhastācchuktikāyāmapāste śītairdravyairañjanaṃ kāryamāśu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.15"><label>ut.10.15</label> vaidūryaṃ yat sphāṭikaṃ vaidrumaṃ
                        ca mauktaṃ śāṅkhaṃ rājataṃ śātakumbham |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ śarkarākṣaudrayuktaṃ śuktiṃ hanyādañjanaṃ caitadāśu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.10.16"><label>ut.10.16</label> yuñjyāt sarpirdhūmadarśī narastu
                        śeṣaṃ kuryād raktapitte vidhānam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yac caivānyat pittahṛc cāpi sarvaṃ yadvīsarpe paittike vai vidhānam ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        pittābhiṣyandapratiṣedho nāma daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||10 ||</p>

                <div n="11" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.3"><label>ut.11.3</label> syandādhimanthau kaphajau

                         svedāvapīḍāñjanadhūmasekapralepayogaiḥ kavalagrahaiś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.4"><label>ut.11.4</label> rūkṣais tathāś cyotanasaṃvidhānais

                        <caesura/>
                         tryahāt tryahāc cāpy apatarpaṇānte prātastayostiktaghṛtaṃ praśastam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.5"><label>ut.11.5</label> tad annapānaṃ ca samācared dhi yac
                        chleṣmaṇo naiva karoti vṛddhim |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuṭannaṭāsphoṭaphaṇijjñabilvapattūrapilvarkakapitthabhaṅgaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.6"><label>ut.11.6</label> svedaṃ vidadhyāt athavānulepaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.7"><label>ut.11.7</label> piṣṭairjalenāñjanavartayaḥ syuḥ
                        pathyāharidrāmadhukāñjanair vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         trīṇyūṣaṇāni triphalā haridrā viḍaṅgasāraś ca samāni ca syuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.8"><label>ut.11.8</label>
                        barhiṣṭhakuṣṭhāmarakāṣṭhaśaṅkhapāṭhāmalavyoṣamanaḥśilāś ca<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭvāmbunā vā kusumāni jātikarañjaśobhāñjanajāni yuñjyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.9"><label>ut.11.9</label> phalaṃ prakīryādathavāpi śigroḥ
                        puṣpaṃ ca tulyaṃ bṛhatīdvayasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāñjanaṃ saindhavacandanaṃ ca manaḥśilāle laśunaṃ ca tulyam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.10"><label>ut.11.10</label> piṣṭvāñjanārthe kaphajeṣu dhīmān
                        vartīrvidadhyānnayanāmayeṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         roge balāsagrathite 'ñjanaṃ jñaiḥ kartavyametat suviśuddhakāye || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.11"><label>ut.11.11</label> nīlān yavān gavyapayo 'nupītān
                        śalākinaḥ śuṣkatanūn vidahya |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathārjakāsphotakapitthabilvanirguṇḍijātīkusumāni caiva || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.12"><label>ut.11.12</label> tatkṣāravatsaindhavatuttharocanaṃ
                        pakvaṃ vidadhyādatha lohanāḍyām |
                        <caesura/>
                         etadbalāsagrathite 'ñjanaṃ syādeṣo 'nukalpas tu phaṇijjñakādau || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.13"><label>ut.11.13</label> mahauṣadhaṃ māgadhikāṃ ca mustāṃ
                        sasaindhavaṃ yanmaricaṃ ca śuklam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tanmātuluṅgasvarasena piṣṭaṃ netrāñjanaṃ piṣṭakamāśu hanyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.14"><label>ut.11.14</label> phale bṛhatyā magadhodbhavānā
                        nidhāya kalkaṃ phalapākakāle |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotojayuktaṃ ca tad uddhṛtaṃ syāt tadvat tu piṣṭe vidhir eṣa cāpi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.15"><label>ut.11.15</label>
                        vārtākaśigrvindrasurāpaṭolakirātatiktāmalakīphaleṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsasāmudrarasāñjanāni jātyās tathā kṣārakam(korakam)eva cāpi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.16"><label>ut.11.16</label> praklinnavartmanyupadiśyate tu
                        yogāñjanaṃ tanmadhunāvaghṛṣṭam |
                        <caesura/>
                         nādeyamagryaṃ maricaṃ ca śuklaṃ nepālajātā ca samapramāṇā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.17"><label>ut.11.17</label> samātuluṅgadrava eṣa yogaḥ kaṇḍūṃ
                        nihanyāt sakṛdañjanena |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśṛṅgaveraṃ suradāru mustaṃ sindhuprabhūtaṃ(prasūtaṃ) mukulāni jātyāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.11.18"><label>ut.11.18</label> surāprapiṣṭaṃ tv idam añjanaṃ hi
                        kaṇḍvāṃ ca śophe ca hitaṃ vadanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         syandādhimanthakramamācarec ca sarveṣu caiteṣu sadāpramattaḥ || (viśeṣato
                        nāvanam eva kāryaṃ saṃsarjanaṃ cāpi yathopadiṣṭam<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>)</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        kaphābhiṣyandapratiṣedho nāmaikādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||11 ||</p>
