                <div n="12" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.1"><label>ut.12.1</label> athāto raktābhiṣyandapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.2"><label>ut.12.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.3"><label>ut.12.3</label> manthaṃ syandaṃ sirotpātaṃ
                        sirāharṣaṃ ca raktajam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekenaiva vidhānena cikitsec caturo gadān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.4"><label>ut.12.4</label> vyādhyārtāṃś caturo 'pyetān
                        snigdhānkaumbhena sarpiṣā |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasair udārair athavā sirāmokṣeṇa yojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.5"><label>ut.12.5</label> viriktānāṃ prakāmaṃ ca śirāṃsy eṣāṃ
                        viśodhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vairecanikasiddhena sitāyuktena sarpiṣā || (majjñā vā tadvimiśreṇa medasā
                        tacchṛtena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ) </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.6"><label>ut.12.6</label> tataḥ pradehāḥ pariṣecanāni nasyāni
                        dhūmāś ca yathāsvam eva |
                        <caesura/>
                         āś cyotanābhyañjanatarpaṇāni snigdhāś ca kāryāḥ puṭapākayogāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.7"><label>ut.12.7</label>
                        nīlotpalośīrakaṭaṅkaṭerīkālīyayaṣṭīmadhumustarodhraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sapadmakairdhautaghṛtapradigdhairakṣṇoḥ pralepaṃ paritaḥ pra kuryāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.8"><label>ut.12.8</label> rujāyāṃ cāpy atibhṛśaṃ svedāś ca
                        mṛdavo hitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         akṣṇoḥ samantataḥ kāryaṃ pātanaṃ ca jalaukasām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.9"><label>ut.12.9</label> ghṛtasya mahatī mātrā pītā cārtiṃ
                        niyacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittābhiṣyandaśamano vidhiś cāpy upapāditaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.10"><label>ut.12.10</label> kaśerumadhukābhyāṃ vā
                        cūrṇamambarasaṃvṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         nyastamapsvāntarikṣāsu hitamāś cyotanaṃ bhavet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.11"><label>ut.12.11</label>
                        pāṭalyarjunaśrīparṇīdhātakīdhātribilvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         puṣpāṇyatha bṛhatyoś ca bimbīloṭāc ca tulyaśaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.12"><label>ut.12.12</label> samañjiṣṭhāni madhunā
                        piṣṭānīkṣurasena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktābhiṣyandaśāntyarthametadañjanamiṣyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.13"><label>ut.12.13</label> candanaṃ kumudaṃ patraṃ śilājatu
                        sakuṅkumam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ayastāmrarajastutthaṃ nimbaniryāsamañjanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.14"><label>ut.12.14</label> trapu kāṃsyamalaṃ cāpi piṣṭvā
                        puṣparasena tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         vipulā yāḥ kṛtā vartyaḥ pūjitāś cāñjane sadā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.15"><label>ut.12.15</label> syādañjanaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣaudraṃ
                        sirotpātasya bheṣajam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadvatsaindhavakāsīsaṃ stanyaghṛṣṭaṃ ca pūjitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.16"><label>ut.12.16</label> madhunā
                        śaṅkhanaipālītutthadārvyaḥ sasaindhavāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasaḥ śirīṣapuṣpāc ca surāmaricamākṣikaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.17"><label>ut.12.17</label> yuktaṃ tu madhunā vāpi gairikaṃ
                        hitamañjane |
                        <caesura/>
                         sirāharṣe 'ñjanaṃ kuryāt phaṇitaṃ madhusaṃyutam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.18"><label>ut.12.18</label> madhunā tārkṣyajaṃ vāpi kāsīaṃ vā
                        sasaidhavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vetrāmlastanyasaṃyuktaṃ phāṇitaṃ ca sasaindhavam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.19"><label>ut.12.19</label> paittaṃ vidhimaśeṣeṇa kuryād
                        arjunaśāntaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         ikṣukṣaudrasitāstanyadārvīmadhukasaindhavaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.20"><label>ut.12.20</label> sekāñjanaṃ cātra hitamamlairāś
                        cyotanaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sitāmadhukakaṭvaṅgamastukṣaudrāmlasaindhavaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.21"><label>ut.12.21</label> bījapūrakakolāmladāḍimāmlaiś ca
                        yuktitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaśo vā dviśo vāpi yojitaṃ vā tribhis tribhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.22"><label>ut.12.22</label> sphaṭikaṃ vidrumaṃ śaṅkho
                        madhukaṃ kadhu caiva hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         śaṅkhakṣaudrasitāyuktaḥ sāmudraḥ phena eva vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.23"><label>ut.12.23</label> dvāvimau vihitau yogāvañjane
                        'rjunanāśanau |
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavakṣaudrakatakāḥ sakṣaudraṃ vā rasāñjanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.24"><label>ut.12.24</label> kāsīsaṃ madhunā vāpi
                        yojyamatrāñjane sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         lohacūrṇāni sarvāṇi dhātavo lavaṇāni ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.25"><label>ut.12.25</label> ratnāni dantāḥ śṛṅgāṇi gaṇaś cāpy
                        avasādanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kukkuṭāṇḍakapālāni laśunaṃ kaṭukatrayam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.26"><label>ut.12.26</label> karañjabījamelā ca
                        lekhyāñjanamidaṃ smṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         puṭapākāvasānena raktavisrāvaṇādinā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.27"><label>ut.12.27</label> saṃpāditasya vidhinā kṛtsnena
                        syandaghātinā |
                        <caesura/>
                         anenāpaharec chukramavraṇaṃ kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.28"><label>ut.12.28</label> uttānamavagāḍhaṃ vā karkaśaṃ vāpi
                        savraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirīṣabījamaricapippalīsaindhavair api || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.29"><label>ut.12.29</label> śukrasya gharṣaṇaṃ kāryamathavā
                        saindhavena tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāt tāmrarajaḥśaṅkhaśilāmaricasaindhavaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.30"><label>ut.12.30</label> antyāddviguṇitairebhir añjanaṃ
                        śukranāśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryād añjanayogau vā samyak ślokārdhikāvimau || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.31"><label>ut.12.31</label>
                        śaṅkhakolāsthikatakadrāksāmadhukamākṣikaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudradantārṇavamalaśirīṣakusumair api || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.32"><label>ut.12.32</label> kṣārāñjanaṃ vā
                        vitaredbalāsagrathitāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         mudgān vā nistuṣān bhṛṣṭān śaṅkhakṣaudrasitāyutān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.33"><label>ut.12.33</label> madhūkasāraṃ madhunā
                        yojayeccāñjane sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bibhītakāsthimajjā vā sakṣaudraḥ śukranāśanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.34"><label>ut.12.34</label> śaṅkhaśuktimadhudrākṣāmadhukaṃ
                        katakāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dvitvaggate saśūle vā vātaghnaṃ tarpaṇaṃ hitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.35"><label>ut.12.35</label> vaṃśajāruṣkarau tālaṃ nārikelaṃ
                        ca dāhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvya ksāravaccūrṇaṃ bhāvayetkarabhāsthijam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.36"><label>ut.12.36</label> bahuśo
                        'ñjanametatsyācchukravaivarṇyanāśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajakāṃ pārśvato viddhvā sūcyā visrāvya codakam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.37"><label>ut.12.37</label> vraṇaṃ gomāṃsacūrṇena pūrayet
                        sarpiṣā saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         bahuśo 'valikhec cāpi vartmāsyopagataṃ yadi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.38"><label>ut.12.38</label> saśophaś cāpy aśophaś ca dvau
                        pākau yau prakīrtitau |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehasvedopapannasya tatra viddhvā sirāṃ bhiṣak || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.39"><label>ut.12.39</label> sekāś cyotananasyāni puṭapākāṃś
                        ca kārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvataś cāpi śuddhasya kartavyamidamañjanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.40"><label>ut.12.40</label> tāmrapātrasthitaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>māsaṃ sarpiḥ saindhavasaṃyutam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         maireyaṃ vāpi dadhyevaṃ dadhyuttarakam eva vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.41"><label>ut.12.41</label> ghṛtaṃ kāṃsyamalopetaṃ stanyaṃ
                        vāpi sasaindhavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhūkasāraṃ madhunā tulyāṃśaṃ gairikeṇa vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.42"><label>ut.12.42</label> sarpiḥsaindhavatāmrāṇi
                        yoṣitstanyayutāni vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāḍimārevatāśmantakolāmlaiś ca sasaindhavām |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakriyāṃ vā vitaretsamyakpākajighāṃsayā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.43"><label>ut.12.43</label> māsaṃ saindhavasaṃyuktaṃ sthitaṃ
                        sarpiṣi nāgaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         āś cyotanāñjanaṃ yojyamabalākṣīrasaṃyutam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.44"><label>ut.12.44</label> jātyāḥ puṣpaṃ saindhavaṃ
                        śṛṅgaveraṃ kṛṣṇābījaṃ kīṭaśatroś ca sāram |
                        <caesura/>
                         etat piṣṭaṃ netrapāke 'ñjanārthaṃ kṣaudropetaṃ nirviśaṅkaṃ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> prayojyam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.45"><label>ut.12.45</label> pūyālase śoṇitamokṣaṇaṃ ca hitaṃ
                        tathaivāpyupanāhanaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtsno vidhiś cekṣaṇapākaghātī yathāvidhānaṃ bhiṣajā prayojyaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.46"><label>ut.12.46</label> kāsīsasindhuprabhavārdrakaistu
                        hitaṃ bhavedañjanam eva cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudrānvitair ebhir athopayuñjyād anyat tu tāmrāyasacūrṇayuktaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.47"><label>ut.12.47</label> snehādibhiḥ samyag apāsya
                        doṣāṃstṛptiṃ vidhāyātha yathāsvam eva |
                        <caesura/>
                         praklinnavartmānam upakrameta sekāñjanāś cyotananasyadhūmaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.48"><label>ut.12.48</label>
                        mustāharidrāmadhukapriyaṅgusiddhārtharodhrotpalasārivābhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣuṇṇābhir āś cyotanam eva kāryamatrāñjanaṃ cāñjanamākṣikaṃ syāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.49"><label>ut.12.49</label> patraṃ phalaṃ cāmalakasya paktvā
                        kriyāṃ vidadhyādathavāñjanārthe |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaṃśasya bhūlena rasakriyāṃ vā vartīkṛtāṃ tāmrakapālapakvām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.50"><label>ut.12.50</label> rasakriyāṃ vā triphalāvipakvāṃ
                        palāśapuṣpaiḥ svaramañjarervā |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭvā chagalyāḥ payasā malaṃ vā kāṃsasya dagdhvā saha tāntavena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.51ab"><label>ut.12.51</label> pratyañjanaṃ tan maricair
                        upetaṃ cūrṇena tāmrasya sahopayojyam |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.51cd"> samudraphenaṃ lavaṇottamaṃ ca śaṅkho 'tha mudgo
                        maricaṃ ca śuklam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.52ab"><label>ut.12.52</label> cūrṇāñjanaṃ jāḍyam athāpi
                        kaṇḍūm aklinnavartmāny upahanti śīghram |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.52cd"> praklinnavartmany api caita eva yogāḥ prayojyāś ca
                        samīkṣya doṣam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.12.53"><label>ut.12.53</label> sakajjalaṃ tāmraghaṭe ca ghṛṣṭaṃ
                        sarpiryutaṃ tulthakam añjanaṃ ca ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        raktābhiṣyandapratiṣedho nāma dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||12 ||</p>
                </div>
                <div n="13" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.1"><label>ut.13.1</label> athāto lekhyarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.2"><label>ut.13.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.3"><label>ut.13.3</label> nava ye 'bhihitā lekhyāḥ
                        sāmānyasteṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhavāntaviriktasya nivātātapasadmani || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.4"><label>ut.13.4</label> (āptair dṛḍhaṃ gṛhītasya veśmany
                        uttānaśāyinaḥ |)
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhodakaprataptena vāsasā susamāhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedayed vartma nirbhujya vāmāṅguṣṭhāṅgulishtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.5"><label>ut.13.5</label> aṅgulyaṅguṣṭhakābhyāṃ tu nirbhugnaṃ
                        vartma yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         plotāntarābhyāṃ na yathā calati sraṃsate 'pi vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.6ab"><label>ut.13.6</label> tataḥ pramṛjya plotena vartma
                        śastrapadāṅkitam |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.6cd"> likhec chastreṇa patrair vā tato rakte sthite punaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.7ab"><label>ut.13.7</label> svinnaṃ
                        manohvākāsīsavyoṣārdrāñjanasaindhavaiḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.7cd"> ślakṣṇapiṣṭaiḥ samākṣīkaiḥ pratisāryoṣṇavāriṇā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.8ab"><label>ut.13.8</label> prakṣālya haviṣā siktaṃ vraṇavat
                        samupācaret |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.8cd"> svedāvapīḍaprabhṛtīṃs tryahād ūrdhvaṃ prayojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.9ab"><label>ut.13.9</label> vyāsataste samuddiṣṭaṃ vidhānaṃ
                        lekhyakarmaṇi |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.9cd"> asṛgāsrāvarahitaṃ kaṇḍūśophavivarjitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.10"><label>ut.13.10</label> samaṃ nakhanibhaṃ vartma likhitaṃ
                        samyag iṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktam akṣi sravet skannaṃ kṣatāc chastrakṛtād dhruvam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.11ab"><label>ut.13.11</label> rāgaśophaparisrāvās timiraṃ
                        vyādhyanirjayaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.11cd"> vartma śyāvaṃ guru stabdhaṃ kaṇḍūharṣopadehavat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.12ab"><label>ut.13.12</label> netrapākam udīrṇaṃ vā
                        kurvītāpratikāriṇaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.12cd"> etad durlikhitaṃ jñeyaṃ snehayitvā punar likhet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.13"><label>ut.13.13</label> vyāvartate yadā vartma pakṣma
                        cāpi vimuhyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         syāt saruk srāvabahulaṃ tadatisrāvitaṃ viduḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.14"><label>ut.13.14</label> snehasvedādiriṣṭaḥ syāt
                        kramastatrānilāpahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vartmāvabandhaṃ kliṣṭaṃ ca bahalaṃ yac ca kīrtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.15"><label>ut.13.15</label> pothakīś cāpy avalikhet
                        pracchayitvāgrataḥ śanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samaṃ likhet tu medhāvī śyāvakardamavartmanī || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.16"><label>ut.13.16</label> kumbhīkinīṃ śarkarāṃ ca
                        tathaivotsaṅginīm api |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalpayitvā tu śastreṇa likhet paś cād atandritaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.17"><label>ut.13.17</label> bhaveyurvartmasu ca yāḥ piḍakāḥ
                        kaṭhinā bhṛśam |
                        <caesura/>
                         hrasvāstāmrāś ca tāḥ pakvā bhindyādbhinnā likhedapi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.13.18"><label>ut.13.18</label> taruṇīś cālpasaṃrambhā piḍakā
                        bāhyavartmajāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viditvaitāḥ praśamayet svedālepanaśodhanaiḥ ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        lekhyarogapratiṣedho nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||13 ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.1"><label>ut.14.1</label> athāto bhedyarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.2"><label>ut.14.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.3"><label>ut.14.3</label> svedayitvā bisagranthiṃ
                        chidrāṇyasya nirāśayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvaṃ bhittvā tu śastreṇa sindhavenāvacūrṇayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.4ab"><label>ut.14.4</label> kāsīsamāgadhīpuṣpanepālyelāyutena
                        tu |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.4cd"> tataḥ kṣaudraghṛtaṃ dattvā samyag bandhamathācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.5"><label>ut.14.5</label> rocanākṣāratutthāni pippalyaḥ
                        kṣaudram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisāraṇamekaikaṃ bhinne lagaṇa iṣyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.6ab"><label>ut.14.6</label> mahaty api ca yuñjīta kṣārāgnī
                        vidhikovidaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.6cd"> svinnāṃ bhinnāṃ viniṣpīḍya bhiṣagañjananāmikām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.7ab"><label>ut.14.7</label> śilailānatasindhūtthaiḥ
                        sakṣaudraiḥ pratisārayet |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.7cd"> rasāñjanamadhubhyāṃ tu bhittvā vā śastrakarmavit || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.8"><label>ut.14.8</label> pratisāryāñjanair yuñjyā duṣṇair
                        dīpaśikhodbhavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaksvinne kṛmigranthau bhinne syāt pratisāraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.9"><label>ut.14.9</label> triphalātutthakāsīsasaindhavaiś ca
                        rasakriyā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhittvopanāhaṃ kaphajaṃ pippalīmadhusaindhavaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.10"><label>ut.14.10</label> lekhayen maṇḍalāgreṇa samantāt
                        pracchayed api |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsnehya patrabhaṅgaiś ca svedayitvā yathāsukham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.14.11"><label>ut.14.11</label> sarveṣveteṣu vihitaṃ vidhānaṃ
                        snehapūrvakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃpakve prayato bhūtvā kurvīta vraṇaropaṇam ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        bhedyarogapratiṣedho nāma caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||14 ||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="15" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.1"><label>ut.15.1</label> athātaś chedyarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.2"><label>ut.15.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.3"><label>ut.15.3</label> snigdhaṃ bhuktavato hy annam
                        upaviṣṭasya yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃroṣayet tu nayanaṃ bhiṣak cūrṇais tu lāvaṇaiḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.4"><label>ut.15.4</label> tataḥ saṃroṣitaṃ tūrṇaṃ susvinnaṃ
                        paridhaṭṭitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         arma yatra valījātaṃ tatraitallagayed bhiṣak || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.5"><label>ut.15.5</label> apāṅgaṃ prekṣamāṇasya baḍiśena
                        samāhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mucuṇḍyādāya medhāvī sūcīsūtreṇa vā punaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.6"><label>ut.15.6</label> na cotthāpayatā kṣipraṃ
                        kāryamabhyunnataṃ tu tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         śastrābādhabhayāccāsya vartmanī grāhayed dṛḍham || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.7"><label>ut.15.7</label> tataḥ praśithilībhūtaṃ tribhir eva
                        vilambitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ullikhanmaṇḍalāgreṇa tīkṣṇena pariśodhayet || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.8"><label>ut.15.8</label> vimuktaṃ sarvataś cāpi
                        kṛṣṇācchuklāc ca maṇḍalāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         nītvā kanīnakopāntaṃ chindyānnātikanīnakam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.9"><label>ut.15.9</label> caturbhāgasthite māṃse nākṣi
                        vyāpattimṛcchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kanīnakavadhādasraṃ nāḍī vāpyupajāyate || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.10"><label>ut.15.10</label> hīnacchedāt punarvṛddhiṃ
                        śīgramevādhigacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         arma yajjālavadvyāpi tadapyunmārjya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> lambitam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.11"><label>ut.15.11</label> chindyādvakreṇa śastreṇa
                        vartmaśuklāntamāthitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisāraṇamakṣṇos tu tataḥ kāryamanantaram || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.12"><label>ut.15.12</label> yāvanālasya cūrṇena
                        trikaṭorlavaṇasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedayitvā tataḥ paś cādbadhnīyāt kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.13"><label>ut.15.13</label> doṣartubalakālajñaḥ snehaṃ dattvā
                        yathāhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇavat saṃvidhānaṃ tu tasya kuryād ataḥ param || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.14"><label>ut.15.14</label> tryahānmuktvā karasvedaṃ dattvā
                        śodhanamācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         karañjabījāmalakamadhukaiḥ sādhitaṃ payaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.15"><label>ut.15.15</label> hitamāś cyotanaṃ śūle dvirahnaḥ
                        kṣaudrasaṃyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhukotpalakiñjalkadūrvākalkaiś ca mūrdhani || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.16"><label>ut.15.16</label> pralepaḥ saghṛtaḥ śītaḥ
                        kṣīrapiṣṭaḥ praśasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         lekhyāñjanair apahared armaśeṣaṃ bhaved yadi || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.17"><label>ut.15.17</label> arma cālpaṃ dadhinibhaṃ nīlaṃ
                        raktam athāpi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūsaraṃ tanu yac cāpi śukravattadupācaret || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.18"><label>ut.15.18</label> carmābhaṃ bahulaṃ yattu
                        snāyumāṃsaghanāvṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         chedyam eva tadarma syāt kṛṣṇamaṇḍalagaṃ ca yat || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.19"><label>ut.15.19</label> viśuddhavarṇam akliṣṭaṃ
                        kriyāsvakṣi gataklamam |
                        <caesura/>
                         chinne 'rmaṇi bhavet samyag yathāsvamanupadravam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.20"><label>ut.15.20</label> sirājāle sirā yās tu kaṭhināstāś
                        ca buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         ullikhenmaṇḍalāgreṇa baḍiśenāvalambitāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.21"><label>ut.15.21</label> sirāsu piḍakā jātā yā na
                        sidhyanti bheṣajaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         armavan maṇḍalāgreṇa tāsāṃ chedanamiṣyate || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.22"><label>ut.15.22</label> rogayoś caitayoḥ kāryamarmoktaṃ
                        pratisāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhiś cāpi yathādoṣaṃ lekhanadravyasaṃbhṛtaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.23"><label>ut.15.23</label> sandhau saṃsvedya śastreṇa
                        varṇīkāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttare ca tribhāge ca baḍiśenāvalambitām || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.24"><label>ut.15.24</label> chindyāttato 'rdhamagre syād
                        aśrunāḍī hy ato 'nyathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisāraṇam atrāpi saindhavakṣaudramiṣyate || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.25"><label>ut.15.25</label> lekhanīyāni cūrṇāni vyādhiśeṣasya
                        bheṣajam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śaṅkhaṃ samudraphenaṃ ca maṇḍūkīṃ ca samudrajām || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.26"><label>ut.15.26</label> sphaṭikaṃ kuruvindaṃ ca
                        pravālāśmantakaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidūryaṃ pulakaṃ muktāmayas tāmrarajāṃsi ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.27"><label>ut.15.27</label> samabhāgāni saṃpiṣya sārdhaṃ
                        srotoñjanena tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇāñjanaṃ kārayitvā bhājane bheṣaśṛṅgaje || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.28"><label>ut.15.28</label> saṃsthāpyobhayataḥ kālamañjayet
                        satataṃ budhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         armāṇi piḍakāṃ hanyāt sirājālāni tena vai || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.29"><label>ut.15.29</label> arśas tathā yac ca nāmnā śuṣkārśo
                        'rbudam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhyantaraṃ vartmaśayā vidhānaṃ teṣu vakṣyate || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.30"><label>ut.15.30</label> vartmopasvedya nirbhujya
                        sūcyotkṣipya prayatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         maṇḍalāgreṇa tīkṣṇena mūle bhindyād bhiṣagvaraḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.31"><label>ut.15.31</label> tataḥ saindhavakāsīsakṛṣṇābhiḥ
                        pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthite ca rudhire vartma dahet samyak śalākayā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.32"><label>ut.15.32</label> kṣāreṇāvalikhec cāpi vyādhiśeso
                        bhaved yadi |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇair ubhayatobhāgais tato doṣam adhikṣipet || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.15.33"><label>ut.15.33</label> vitarec ca yathādoṣam
                        abhiṣyandakriyāvidhim |
                        <caesura/>
                         śastrakarmaṇy uparate māsaṃ ca syāt suyantritaḥ ||</l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        chedyarogapratiṣedho nāma pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||15 ||</p>
                </div>



                <div n="16" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.1"><label>ut.16.1</label> athātaḥ <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>pakṣmakopapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.2"><label>ut.16.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.3"><label>ut.16.3</label> yāpyas tu yo vartmabhavo vikāraḥ
                        pakṣmaprakopo 'bhihitaḥ purastāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatropaviṣṭasya narasya carma vartmopariṣṭād anutiryag eva || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.4ab"><label>ut.16.4</label> bhruvor adhastāt parimucya bhāgau
                        pakṣmāśritaṃ caikam ato 'vakṛntet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.4cd"> kanīnakāpāṅgasamaṃ samantād yavākṛti snigdhatanor
                        narasya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.5"><label>ut.16.5</label> utkṛtya śastreṇa yavapramāṇaṃ
                        bālena sīvyodbhiṣagapramattaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dattvā ca sarpirmadhunāvaśeṣaṃ kuryād vidhānaṃ vihitaṃ vraṇe yat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.6ab"><label>ut.16.6</label> lalāṭadeśe ca nibaddhapaṭṭaṃ prāk
                        syūtam atrāpy aparaṃ ca baddhvā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.6cd"> sthairyaṃ gate cāpy atha śastramārge bālān vimuñcet
                        kuśalo 'bhivīkṣya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.7"><label>ut.16.7</label> evaṃ na cec chāmyati tasya vartma
                        nirbhujya doṣopahatāṃ valiṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato 'gninā vā pratisārayettāṃ kṣāreṇa vā samyag avekṣya dhīraḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.8"><label>ut.16.8</label> chittvā samaṃ vāpyupapakṣmamālāṃ
                        samyag gṛhītvā baḍiśaistribhis tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyāphalena pratisārayet tu ghṛṣṭena vā tauvarakeṇa samyak || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.16.9"><label>ut.16.9</label> catvāra ete vidhayo vihantuṃ
                        pakṣmoparodhaṃ pṛthageva śastāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanāś cyotanadhūmanasyalepāñjanasneharasakriyāś ca ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        pakṣmagatarogapratiṣedho nāma ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||16 ||</p>

                         meṣasya puṣpair madhukena saṃyutaṃ tad añjanaṃ sarvakṛte prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.18.103"><label>ut.18.103</label> kāṃsyāpamārjanamasī madhukaṃ
                        saindhavaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         eraṇḍamūlaṃ ca samaṃ bṛhatyaṃśadvayānvitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.18.104"><label>ut.18.104</label> ājena payasā piṣṭvā tāmrapātraṃ
                        pralepayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         saptakṛtvas tu tā vartyaś chāyāśuṣkā rujāpahāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.18.105"><label>ut.18.105</label>
                        pathyātutthakayaṣṭyāhvaistulyairmaricaṣoḍaśā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyā sarvavikāreṣu vartiḥ śītāmbupeṣitā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.18.106"><label>ut.18.106</label> rasakriyāvidhānena
                        yathoktavidhikovidaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṇḍāñjanāni kurvīta yathāyogamatandritaḥ ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        kriyākalpo nāmāṣṭadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||18 ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="20" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> viṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.1"><label>ut.20.1</label> athātaḥ
                        karṇagatarogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.2"><label>ut.20.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.3"><label>ut.20.3</label> karṇaśūlaṃ praṇādaś ca bādhiryaṃ
                        kṣveḍa eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇasrāvaḥ karṇakaṇḍūḥ karṇavarcas tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.4"><label>ut.20.4</label> kṛmikarṇapratināhau
                        vidradhirdvividhas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇapākaḥ pūtikarṇastathaivārśaś caturvidham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.5"><label>ut.20.5</label> karṇārbudaṃ saptavidhaṃ śophaś cāpi
                        caturvidhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete karṇagatā rogā aṣṭāviṃśatirīritāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.6"><label>ut.20.6</label> samīraṇaḥ śrotragato 'nyathācaraḥ
                        samantataḥ śūlamatīva karṇayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karoti doṣaiś ca yathāsvamāvṛtaḥ sa karṇaśūlaḥ kathito durācaraḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.7"><label>ut.20.7</label> yadā tu nāḍīṣu vimārgamāgataḥ sa
                        eva śabdābhivahāsu tiṣṭhati |
                        <caesura/>
                         śrṇoti śabdān vividhāṃstadā naraḥ praṇādamenaṃ kathayanti cāmayam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.8"><label>ut.20.8</label> sa eva śabdānuvahā yadā sirāḥ
                        kaphānuyāto vyanusṛtya tiṣṭhati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā narasyāpratikārasevino bhavet tu bādhiryamasaṃśayaṃ khalu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.9"><label>ut.20.9</label> śramāt kṣayādrūkṣakaṣāyabhojanāt
                        samīraṇaḥ śabdapathe pratiṣṭhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viriktaśīrṣasya ca śītasevinaḥ karoti hi kṣveḍamatīva karṇayoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.10"><label>ut.20.10</label> śirobhighātād athavā nimajjato
                        jale prapākādayavāpi vidradheḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sravet tu pūyaṃ śravaṇo 'nilāvṛtaḥ sa karṇasaṃsrāva iti prakīrtitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.11"><label>ut.20.11</label> kaphena kaṇḍūḥ pracitena karṇayor
                        bhṛśaṃ bhavet srotasi karṇasaṃjñite |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśoṣite śleṣmaṇi pittatejasā nṛṇāṃ bhavet srotasi karṇagūthakaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.12"><label>ut.20.12</label> sa karṇaviṭko dravatāṃ yadā gato
                        vilāyito ghrāṇamukhaṃ prapadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā sa karṇapratināhasaṃjñito bhaved vikāraḥ śiraso 'bhitāpanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.13"><label>ut.20.13</label> yadā tu mūrcchanty athavāpi
                        jantavaḥ sṛjanty apatyānyathavāpi makṣikāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadañjanatvāc chravaṇo nirucyate bhiṣagbhir ādyaiḥ kṛmikarṇako gadaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.14"><label>ut.20.14</label> kṣatābhighātaprabhavas tu
                        vidradhir bhavet tathā doṣakṛto 'paraḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saraktapītāruṇam asram āsravet pratodadhūmāyanadāhacopavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.15"><label>ut.20.15</label> bhavet prapākaḥ khalu pittakopato
                        vikothavikledakaraś ca karṇayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthite kaphe srotasi pittatejasaḥ vilāyyamāne bhṛśasaṃpratāpavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.16"><label>ut.20.16</label> avedano vāpy athavā savedano
                        ghanaṃ sravet pūti ca pūtikarṇakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradiṣṭaliṅgānyaraśāṃsi tattvatas tathaiva śophārbudaliṅgamīritam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mayā purastāt prasamīkṣya yojayed ihaiva tāvat prayato bhiṣagvaraḥ ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        karṇagatarogavijñānīyo nāma viṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||20 ||</p>
                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.20"><label>ut.21.20</label> mahataḥ pañcamūlasya

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.22"><label>ut.21.22</label> kuryād evaṃ bhadrakāṣṭhe kuṣṭhe

                         samudraphenacūrṇena yuktyā cāpy avacūrṇayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.27"><label>ut.21.27</label> aṣṭānāmiha mūtrāṇāṃ

                         koṣṇena pūrayet karṇaṃ karṇaśūlopaśāntaye || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.28"><label>ut.21.28</label> mūtreṣv amleṣu vātaghne gaṇe ca
                        kvathite bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         pacec caturvidhaṃ snehaṃ pūraṇaṃ tac ca karṇayoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.29"><label>ut.21.29</label> etā eva kriyāḥ kuryāt pittaghnaiḥ
                        pittasaṃyute |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolyādau daśakṣīraṃ tiktaṃ cātra hitaṃ haviḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.30"><label>ut.21.30</label> kṣīravṛkṣapravāleṣu madhuke
                        candane tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkakvāthe paraṃ pakvaṃ śarkarāmadhukaiḥ saraiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.31"><label>ut.21.31</label> iṅgudīsarṣapasnehau sakaphe
                        pūraṇe hitau |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiktauṣadhānāṃ yūṣāś ca svedāś ca kaphanāśanāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.32"><label>ut.21.32</label> surasādau kṛtaṃ tailaṃ pañcamūle
                        mahatyapi |
                        <caesura/>
                         mātuluṅgarasaḥ śuktaṃ laśunārdrakayo rasaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.33"><label>ut.21.33</label> ekaikaḥ pūraṇe pathyastailaṃ teṣv
                        api vā kṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇā mūrdhavirekāś ca kavalāś cātra pūjitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.34"><label>ut.21.34</label> karṇaśūlavidhiḥ kṛtsnaḥ
                        pittaghnaḥ śoṇitāvṛte |
                        <caesura/>
                         śūlapraṇādabādhiryakṣveḍānāṃ tu prakīrtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.35"><label>ut.21.35</label> sāmānyato viśeṣeṇa<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> bādhirye pūraṇaṃ śṛṇu |
                        <caesura/>
                         gavāṃ mūtreṇa bilvāni piṣṭvā tailaṃ vipācayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.36"><label>ut.21.36</label> sajalaṃ ca sadugdhaṃ ca bādhirye
                        karṇapūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sitāmadhukabimbībhiḥ siddhaṃ vāje payasyapi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.37"><label>ut.21.37</label> bimbīkvāthe vimathyoṣṇaṃ
                        śītībhūtaṃ taduddhṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         punaḥ paceddaśakṣīraṃ sitāmadhukacandanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.38"><label>ut.21.38</label> bilvāmbugāḍhaṃ tattailaṃ bādhirye
                        karṇapūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vakṣyate yaḥ pratiśyāye vidhiḥ so 'pyatra pūjitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.39"><label>ut.21.39</label> vātavyādhiṣu yaś cokto vidhiḥ sa
                        ca hito bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇasrāve pūtikarṇe tathaiva kṛmikarṇake || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.40"><label>ut.21.40</label> samānaṃ karma kurvīta yogān
                        vaiśeṣikānapi |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanaṃ caiva dhūpanaṃ pūraṇaṃ tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.41"><label>ut.21.41</label> pramārjanaṃ dhāvanaṃ ca vīkṣya
                        vīkṣyāvcārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         rājavṛkṣāditoyena surasādigaṇena vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.42"><label>ut.21.42</label> karṇaprakṣālanaṃ kāryaṃ
                        cūrṇaireṣāṃ ca pūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kvāthaṃ pañjcakaṣāyaṃ tu kapittharasayojitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.43"><label>ut.21.43</label> karṇasrāve praśaṃsanti pūraṇaṃ
                        madhunā saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarjatvakcūrṇasaṃyuktaḥ kārpāsīphalajo rasaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.44"><label>ut.21.44</label> yojito madhunā vāpi karṇasrāve
                        praśasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         lākṣā rasāñjanaṃ sarjaś cūrṇitaṃ karṇapūraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.45"><label>ut.21.45</label> saśaivalaṃ
                        mahāvṛkṣajambvāmraprasavāyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulīrakṣaudramaṇḍūkīsiddhaṃ tailaṃ ca pūjitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.46"><label>ut.21.46</label> tindukānyabhayā rodhraṃ
                        samaṅgāmalakaṃ madhu |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūraṇaṃ cātra pathyaṃ syātkapittharasayojitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.47"><label>ut.21.47</label> rasamāmrakapitthānāṃ
                        madhūkadhavaśālajam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūraṇārthaṃ praśaṃsanti tailaṃ vā tairvipācitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.48"><label>ut.21.48</label>
                        priyaṅgumadhukāmbaṣṭhādhātakīśilaparṇibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhālobhralākṣābhiḥ kapitthasya rasena vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.49"><label>ut.21.49</label> pacettailaṃ tadāsrāvamavagṛhṇāti
                        pūraṇāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ rasāñjnaṃ nāryāḥ kṣīreṇa madhusaṃyutam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.50"><label>ut.21.50</label> tatpraśastaṃ cirotthe 'pi sāsrāve
                        pūtikarṇake |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirguṇḍīsvarasastailaṃ sindhurdhūmarajo guḍaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.51"><label>ut.21.51</label> pūraṇaḥ pūtikarṇasya śamano
                        madhusaṃyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛmikarṇakanāśārthaṃ kṛmighnaṃ yojayed vidhim || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.52"><label>ut.21.52</label> vārtākudhūmaś ca hitaḥ
                        sārṣapasneha eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛmighnaṃ haritālena gavāṃ mūtrayutena ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.53"><label>ut.21.53</label> gugguloḥ karṇadaurgandhye
                        dhūpanaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         chardanaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca kavalasya ca dhāraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.54"><label>ut.21.54</label> karṇakṣveḍe hitaṃ tailaṃ sārṣapaṃ
                        caiva pūraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidradhau cāpi kurvīta vidradhyuktaṃ cikitsitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.55"><label>ut.21.55</label> prakledya dhīmāṃstailena svedena
                        pravilāyya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhayetkarṇaviṭkaṃ tu bhiṣak samyak śalākayā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.56"><label>ut.21.56</label> nāḍīsvedo 'tha vamanaṃ dhūmo
                        mūrdhavirecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhiś ca kaphahṛtsarvaḥ karṇakaṇḍūmapohati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.57"><label>ut.21.57</label> atha karṇapratīnāhe snehasvedau
                        prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato viriktaśirasaḥ kriyāṃ prāptāṃ samācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.58"><label>ut.21.58</label> karṇapākasya bhaiṣajyaṃ kuryāt
                        pittavisarpavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇacchidre vartamānaṃ kīṭaṃ kledamalādi vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.21.59"><label>ut.21.59</label> śṛṅgeṇāpahareddhīmānathavāpi
                        śalākayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣāṇāṃ tu vikārāṇāṃ prāk cikitsitamīritam ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        karṇagatarogapratiṣedho nāmaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||21 ||</p>
                </div>
                <div n="22" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.1"><label>ut.22.1</label> athāto
                        nāsāgatarogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.2"><label>ut.22.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.3"><label>ut.22.3</label> apīnasaḥ pūtinasyaṃ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> nāsāpākas tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā śoṇitapittaṃ ca pūyaśoṇitam eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.4"><label>ut.22.4</label> kṣavathurbhraṃśathurdīpto nāsānāhaḥ
                        parisravaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāśoṣeṇa sahitā daśaikāś ceritā gadāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.5"><label>ut.22.5</label> catvāryarśāṃsi catvāraḥ śophāḥ
                        saptārbudāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratiśyāyāś ca ye pañca vakṣyante sacikitsitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekatriṃśanmitāste tu nāsārogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.6"><label>ut.22.6</label> ānahyate yasya vidhūpyate ca
                        praklidyate śuṣyati cāpi nāsā |
                        <caesura/>
                         na vetti yo gandharasāṃś ca janturjuṣṭaṃ vyavasyettamapīnasena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.7"><label>ut.22.7</label> taṃ cānilaśleṣmabhavaṃ vikāraṃ
                        brūyāt pratiśyāyasamānaliṅgam |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣairvidagdhairlatālumūle saṃvāsito yasya samīraṇas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.8"><label>ut.22.8</label> nireti pūtirmukhanāsikābhyāṃ taṃ
                        pūtināsaṃ pravadanti rogam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vrāṇāśritaṃ pittamarūṃṣi kuryād yasmin vikāre balavāṃś ca pākaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.9"><label>ut.22.9</label> taṃ nāsikāpākam iti vyavasyed
                        vikledakothāvapi yatra dṛṣṭau |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvidhaṃ dviprabhavaṃ vakṣyāmi bhūyaḥ khalu raktapittam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.10"><label>ut.22.10</label> doṣairvidagdhairathavāpi
                        jantorlalāṭadeśe 'bhihatasya tais tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsā sravet pūyamasṛgvimiśraṃ taṃ pūyaraktaṃ pravadanti rogam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.11"><label>ut.22.11</label> ghrāṇāśrite marmaṇi saṃpraduṣṭe
                        yasyānilo nāsikayā nireti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.12"><label>ut.22.12</label> kaphānuyāto bahuśaḥ saśabdastaṃ
                        rogam āhuḥ kṣavathuṃ vidhijñāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇopayogādatijighrato vā bhāvān kaṭūnarkanirīkṣaṇādvā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.13"><label>ut.22.13</label> sūtrādibhir vā
                        taruṇāsthimarmaṇyudghāṭite 'nyaḥ kṣavathurnireti |
                        <caesura/>
                         prabhraśyate nāsikayaiva yaś ca<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> sāndro vidagdho lavaṇaḥ kaphas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.14"><label>ut.22.14</label> prāk saṃcito mūrdhani
                        pittataptastaṃ bhraṃśathuṃ vyādhimudāharanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghrāṇe bhṛśaṃ dāhasamanvite tu viniḥsareddhūma iveha vāyuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.15"><label>ut.22.15</label> nāsā pradīpteva ca yasya
                        jantorvyādhiṃ tu taṃ dīptamudāharanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphāvṛto vāyurudānasaṃjño yadā svamārge viguṇaḥ sthitaḥ syāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.16"><label>ut.22.16</label> ghrāṇaṃ vṛṇotīva tadā sa rogo
                        nāsāpratīnāha iti pradiṣṭaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajasramacchaṃ salilaprakāśaṃ yasyāvivarṇe sravatīha nāsā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.17"><label>ut.22.17</label> rātrau viśeṣeṇa hi taṃ vikāraṃ
                        nāsāparisrāvam iti vyavasyet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghrāṇāśrite śleṣmaṇi mārutena pittena gāḍhaṃ pariśoṣite ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.18"><label>ut.22.18</label> samucchvasityūrdhvamadhaś ca
                        kṛcchrādyastasya nāsāpariśoṣa uktaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣaiśtribhis taiḥ pṛthagekaśaś ca brūyāttathārśāṃsi tathaiva śophān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.19"><label>ut.22.19</label> śālākyasiddhāntamavekṣya cāpi
                        sarvātmakaṃ saptamamarbudaṃ tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogaḥ pratiśyāya ihopadiṣṭaḥ sa vakṣyate pañcavidhaḥ purastāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.20"><label>ut.22.20</label> (nāsāsrotogatā rogāstriṃśadekaś
                        ca kīrtitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotaḥpathe yadvipulaṃ kośavaccārbudaṃ bhavet<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> ||) </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.22.21"><label>ut.22.21</label> śophās tu śophavijñānā
                        nāsāsrotovyavasthitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nidāne 'rśāṃsi nirdiṣṭānyevaṃ tāni vibhāvayet ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        nāsāgatarogavijñānīyo nāma dvāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||22 ||</p>
                </div>
                <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.1"><label>ut.23.1</label> athāto nāsāgatarogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.2"><label>ut.23.2</label> athovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.3"><label>ut.23.3</label> pūrvoddiṣṭe pūtinasye ca jantoḥ
                        snehasvedau chardanaṃ sraṃsanaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktaṃ bhaktaṃ tīkṣṇamalpaṃ laghu syāduṣṇaṃ toyaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca kāle || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.4"><label>ut.23.4</label> hiṅgu vyoṣaṃ vatsakākhyaṃ śivāṭī
                        lākṣā bījaṃ saurabhaṃ kaṭphalaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ugrā kuṣṭhaṃ tīkṣṇagandhā viḍaṅgaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nityaṃ cāvapīḍe karañjam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.5"><label>ut.23.5</label> etairdravyaiḥ sārṣapaṃ mūtrayuktaṃ
                        tailaṃ dhīmānnasyahetoḥ paceta |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāpāke pittahṛtsaṃvidhānaṃ kāryaṃ sarvaṃ bāhyamābhyantaraṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.6"><label>ut.23.6</label> hṛtvā raktaṃ kṣīravṛkṣatvacaś ca
                        sājyāḥ sekā yojanīyāś ca lepāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vakṣyāmyūrdhvaṃ raktapītopaśāntiṃ nāḍīvatsyāt pūyarakte cikitsā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.7"><label>ut.23.7</label> vānte samyak cāvapīḍaṃ vadanti
                        tīkṣṇaṃ dhūmaṃ śodhanaṃ cātra nasyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣepyaṃ nasyaṃ mūrdhavairecanīyairnāḍyā cūrṇaṃ kṣavathau bhraṃśathau ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.8"><label>ut.23.8</label> kuryāt svedān mūrdhni vātāmayaghnān
                        snigdhān dhūmān yadyanyaddhitaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dīpte roge paittikaṃ saṃvidhānaṃ kuryāt sarvaṃ svādu yacchītalaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.9"><label>ut.23.9</label> nāsānāhe snehapānaṃ pradhānaṃ
                        snigdhā dhūmā mūrdhabastiś ca nityam |
                        <caesura/>
                         balātailaṃ sarvathaivopayojyaṃ vātavyādhāvanyaduktaṃ ca yadyat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.10"><label>ut.23.10</label> nāsāsrāve ghrāṇataś cūrṇamuktaṃ
                        nāḍyā deyaṃ yo 'vapīḍaś ca tīkṣṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇaṃ dhūmaṃ devadārvagnikābhyāṃ māṃsaṃ vājaṃ yuktamatrādiśanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.11"><label>ut.23.11</label> nāsāśoṣe kṣīrasarpiḥ pradhānaṃ
                        siddhaṃ tailaṃ cāṇukalpena nasyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥpānaṃ bhojanaṃ jāṅgalaiś ca snehaḥ svedaḥ snaihikaś cāpi dhūmaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.23.12"><label>ut.23.12</label> śeṣān rogān ghrāṇajān
                        sanniyaccheduktaṃ teṣāṃ yadyathā saṃvidhānam ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        nāsāgatarogapratiṣedho nāma trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||23 ||</p>
                </div>
                <div n="24" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.1"><label>ut.24.1</label> athātaḥ pratiśyāyapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.2"><label>ut.24.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.3"><label>ut.24.3</label> nārīprasaṅgaḥ śiraso 'bhitāpo dhūmo
                        rajaḥ śītamatipratāpaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃdhāraṇaṃ mūtrapurīṣayoś ca sadyaḥ pratiśyāyanidānamuktam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.4"><label>ut.24.4</label> cayaṃ gatā mūrdhani mārutādayaḥ
                        pṛthak samastāś ca tathaiva śoṇitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakopyamāṇā vividhaiḥ prakopaṇairnṛṇāṃ pratiśyāyakarā bhavanti hi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.5"><label>ut.24.5</label> śirogurutvaṃ kṣavathoḥ pravartanaṃ
                        tathāṅgamardaḥ parihṛṣṭaromatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upadravāś cāpy apare pṛthagvidhā nṛṇāṃ pratiśyāyapuraḥsarāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.6"><label>ut.24.6</label> ānaddhā pihitā nāsā
                        tanusrāvapravartinī |
                        <caesura/>
                         galatālvoṣṭhaśoṣaś ca nistodaḥ śaṅkhayos tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.7"><label>ut.24.7</label> svaropaghātaś ca bhavet pratiśyāye
                        'nilātmake |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇaḥ sapītakaḥ srāvo ghrāṇāt sravati paittike || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.8"><label>ut.24.8</label> kṛśo 'tipāṇḍuḥ santapto
                        bhavettṛṣṇānipīḍitaḥ(tṛṣṇābhipīḍitaḥ) |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadhūmaṃ sahasā vahniṃ vamatīva ca mānavaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.9"><label>ut.24.9</label> kaphaḥ kaphakṛte ghrāṇācchuklaḥ
                        śītaḥ sravenmuhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklāvabhāsaḥ śūnākṣo bhavedguruśiromukhaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.24.10"><label>ut.24.10</label> śirogalauṣṭhatālūnāṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.5"><label>ut.25.5</label> yasyānimittaṃ śiraso rujaś ca
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.6"><label>ut.25.6</label> yasyoṣṇam aṅgāracitaṃ yathaiva
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         śītena rātrau ca bhaved viśeṣaḥ
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.7"><label>ut.25.7</label> śirogalaṃ yasya kaphopadigdhaṃ
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         śūnākṣikūṭaṃ vadanaṃ ca yasya
                        <caesura/>
                         śirobhitāpaḥ sa kaphaprakopāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.8"><label>ut.25.8</label> śirobhitāpe tritayapravṛtte sarvāṇi
                        liṅgāni samudbhavanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktātmakaḥ pittasamānaliṅgaḥ sparśāsahatvaṃ śiraso bhavec ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.9"><label>ut.25.9</label> vasābalāsakṣatasaṃbhavānāṃ
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         kṣayapravṛttaḥ śiraso 'bhitāpaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣṭo bhavedugrarujo 'timātram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.10"><label>ut.25.10</label> saṃsvedanacchardanadhūmanasyair
                        asṛgvimokṣaiś ca vivṛddhim eti |
                        <caesura/>
                         nistudyate yasya śiro 'timātraṃ saṃbhakṣyamāṇaṃ sphuṭatīva cāntaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.11"><label>ut.25.11</label> ghrāṇāc ca gacchetsalilaṃ
                        saraktaṃ śirobhitāpaḥ kṛmibhiḥ sa ghoraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sūryodayaṃ yā prati mandamandamakṣibhruvaṃ ruk samupaiti gāḍham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.12"><label>ut.25.12</label> vivardhate cāṃśumatā sahaiva
                        sūryāpavṛttau vinivartate ca |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.13"><label>ut.25.13</label> taṃ bhāskarāvartam udāharanti
                        sarvātmakaṃ kaṣṭatamaṃ vikāram |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣās tu duṣṭās traya eva manyāṃ saṃpīḍya ghāṭāsu rujāṃ sutīvrām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.14"><label>ut.25.14</label> kurvanti sākṣibhruvi śaṅkhadeśe
                        sthitiṃ karoty āśu viśeṣatas tu |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.15ab"><label>ut.25.15</label> anantavātaṃ tam udāharanti
                        doṣatrayotthaṃ śiraso vikāram |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.15cd"> yasyottamāṅgārdham atīva jantoḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.16"><label>ut.25.16</label> pakṣāddaśāhād athavāpy akasmāt
                        tasyārdham edaṃ tritayād vyavasyet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śaṅkhāśrito vāyur udīrṇavegaḥ kṛtānuyātraḥ kaphapittaraktaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.17"><label>ut.25.17</label> rujaḥ sutīvrāḥ pratanoti mūrdhni
                        viśeṣataś cāpi hi śaṅkhayos tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukaṣṭamenaṃ khalu śaṅkhakākhyaṃ maharṣayo vedavidaḥ purāṇāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.25.18"><label>ut.25.18</label> vyādhiṃ vadanty udgatamṛtyukalpaṃ
                        bhiṣaksahasrair api durnivāram ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.1"><label>ut.26.1</label> athātaḥ śirorogapratiṣedhaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.19cd"> acchaṃ ca pāyayet sarpiḥ svedayec cāpy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.20"><label>ut.26.20</label> śiro madhūkasāreṇa snigdhaṃ cāpi

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.22"><label>ut.26.22</label> saralākuṣṭhaśārṅgeṣṭādevakāṣṭhaiḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.23"><label>ut.26.23</label> yavaṣaṣṭikayoś cānnaṃ

                        <caesura/>
                         paṭolamudgakaulatthairmātrāvadbhojayed rasaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.24"><label>ut.26.24</label> śiroroge tridoṣotthe tridoṣaghno
                        vidhirhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥpānaṃ viśeṣeṇa purāṇaṃ vā diśanti hi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.25"><label>ut.26.25</label> kṣayaje kṣayamāsādya kartavyo
                        bṛṃhaṇo vidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāne nasye ca sarpiḥ syādvātaghnamadhuraiḥ śṛtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.26"><label>ut.26.26</label> kṣayakāsāpahaṃ cātra sarpiḥ
                        pathyatamaṃ viduḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛmibhir bhakṣyamāṇasya vakṣyate śirasaḥ kriyā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.27"><label>ut.26.27</label> nasye hi śoṇitaṃ dadyāttena
                        mūrcchanti jantavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mattāḥ śoṇitagandhena samāyānti yatastataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.28"><label>ut.26.28</label> teṣāṃ nirharaṇaṃ kāryaṃ tato
                        mūrdhavirecanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hrasvaśigrukabījair vā kāṃsyanīlīsamāyutaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.29"><label>ut.26.29</label> kṛmighnairavapīḍaiś ca
                        mūtrapiṣṭair upācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūtimatsyayutān dhūmān kṛmighnāṃś ca prayojayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.30"><label>ut.26.30</label> bhojanāni kṛmighnāni pānāni
                        vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sūryāvarte vidhātavyaṃ nasyakarmādibheṣajam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.31ab"><label>ut.26.31</label> bhojanaṃ jāṅgalaprāyaṃ
                        kṣīrānnavikṛtirghṛtam |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.31cd"> tathārdhabhedake vyādhau prāptam anyac ca yad bhavet
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.32ab"><label>ut.26.32</label> śirīṣamūlakaphalair avapīḍo
                        'nayor hitaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.32cd"> vaṃśamūlakaphalair avapīḍo 'nayor hitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.33A"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.33"><label>ut.26.33</label> avapīḍo hitaś cātra
                        vacāmāgadhikāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.34"><label>ut.26.34</label> manaḥśilāvapīḍo vā madhunā
                        candanena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāmante hitaṃ nasyaṃ sarpirmadhurasānvitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.35"><label>ut.26.35</label> sārivotpalakuṣṭhāni madhukaṃ
                        cāmlapeṣitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpistailayuto lepo dvayor api sukhāvahaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.36"><label>ut.26.36</label> eṣa eva prayoktavyaḥ śiroroge
                        kaphātmake |
                        <caesura/>
                         anantavāte kartavyaḥ sūryāvartaharo<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> vidhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.37ab"><label>ut.26.37</label> sirāvyadhaś ca kartavyo
                        'nantavātapraśāntaye |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.37cd"> āhāraś ca vidhātavyo vātapittavināśanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.38"><label>ut.26.38</label> madhumastakasaṃyāvaghṛtapūraiś ca
                        bhojanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrasarpiḥ praśaṃsanti nasye pāne ca śaṅkhake || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.39"><label>ut.26.39</label> jāṅgalānāṃ rasaiḥ snigdhairāhāraś
                        cātra śasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvarīṃ tilān kṛṣṇān madhukaṃ nīlamutpalam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.40"><label>ut.26.40</label> dūrvāṃ punarnavāṃ caiva lepe
                        sādhv avacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahāsugandhām athavā pālindīṃ cāmlapeṣitām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.41"><label>ut.26.41</label> śītāṃś cātra parīṣekān pradehāṃś
                        ca prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         avapīḍaś ca deyo 'tra sūryāvartanivāraṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.42"><label>ut.26.42</label> kṛmikṣayakṛtau hitvā śirorogeṣu
                        buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhutailasamāyuktaiḥ śirāṃsyativirecayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.43"><label>ut.26.43</label> paś cātsarṣapatailena tato nasyaṃ
                        prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.44"><label>ut.26.44</label> paś cādupācaretsamyak sirāṇāmatha

                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṭsaptatirnetrarogā daśāṣṭādaśa karṇajāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.45"><label>ut.26.45</label> ekatriṃśad ghrāṇagatāḥ
                        śirasyekādaśaiva tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         iti vistarato dṛṣṭāḥ(diṣṭāḥ) salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.26.46"><label>ut.26.46</label> etāvanto
                        yathāsthūlamuttamāṅgagatā gadāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         asmiñchāstre nigaditāḥ saṅkhyārūpacikitsitaiḥ ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        śirorogapratiṣedho nāma ṣaṅviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||26 ||</p>

                <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.1"><label>ut.27.1</label> athāto
                        navagrahākṛtivijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.2"><label>ut.27.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.3"><label>ut.27.3</label> bālagrahāṇāṃ vijñānaṃ sādhanaṃ cāpy
                        anantaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         utpattiṃ kāraṇaṃ caiva suśrutaikamanāḥ śṛṇu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.4"><label>ut.27.4</label> skandagrahas tu prathamaḥ
                        skandāpasmāra eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         śakunī revatī caiva pūtanā cāndhapūtanā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.5"><label>ut.27.5</label> pūtanā śītanāmā ca tathaiva
                        mukhamaṇḍikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         navamo naigameṣaś ca yaḥ pitṛgrahasaṃjñitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.6"><label>ut.27.6</label> dhātrīmātroḥ
                        prākpradiṣṭāpacārācchaucabhraṣṭānmaṅgalācārahīnān |
                        <caesura/>
                         trastān hṛṣṭāṃtarjitān tāḍitān vā pūjāhetorhiṃsyurete kumārān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.7"><label>ut.27.7</label> aiśvaryasthāste na śakyā viśanto
                        dehaṃ draṣṭuṃ mānuṣairviśvarūpāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āptaṃ vākyaṃ tatsamīkṣyābhidhāsye liṅgānyeṣāṃ yāni dehe bhavanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.8"><label>ut.27.8</label> śūnākṣaḥ<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> kṣatajasagandhikaḥ
                        stanadviḍ vakrāsyo hatacalitaikapakṣmanetraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         udvigraḥ sululitacakṣuralparodī skandārto bhavati ca gāḍhamuṣṭivarcāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.9"><label>ut.27.9</label> niḥsaṃjño bhavati punar bhavet
                        sasaṃjñaḥ saṃrabdhaḥ karacaraṇaiś ca nṛtyatīva |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtre sṛjati vinadya jṛmbhamāṇaḥ phenaṃ ca prasṛjati tat sakhābhipannaḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.10"><label>ut.27.10</label> srastāṅgo bhayacakito
                        vihaṅgagandhiḥ saṃsrāvivraṇaparipīḍitaḥ samantāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         sphoṭaiś ca pracitatanuḥ sadāhapākair vijñeyo bhavati śiśuḥ kṣataḥ śakunyā
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.11"><label>ut.27.11</label> raktāsyo haritamalo 'tipāṇḍudehaḥ
                        śyāvo vā jvaramukhapākavedanātaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         revatyā viyathitatanuś ca karṇanāsaṃ mṛdgāti dhruvam abhipīḍitaḥ kumāraḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.12"><label>ut.27.12</label> srastāṅgaḥ svapiti sukhaṃ divā na
                        rātrau viḍ bhinnaṃ sṛjati ca kākatulyagandhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         chardyārto hṛṣitatanūruhaḥ kumāras tṛṣṇālur bhavati ca pūtanāgṛhītaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.13"><label>ut.27.13</label> yo dveṣṭi
                        stanamatisārakāsahikkācchardībhir jvarasahitābhir ardyamānaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         durvarṇaḥ satatam adhaḥśayo 'mlagandhistaṃ brūyur bhiṣaja ihāndhapūtanārtam
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.14"><label>ut.27.14</label> udvigro bhṛśam ativepate
                        prarudyāt saṃlīnaḥ ssvapiti ca yasya cāntrakūjaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāṅgo bhṛśam atisāryate ca yastaṃ jānīyād bhiṣag iha śītapūtanārtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.15"><label>ut.27.15</label> mlānāṅgaḥ surucir apāṇipādavaktro
                        bahvāśī kaluṣasirāvṛtodaro yaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sodvego bhavati ca mūtratulyagandhiḥ sa jñeyaḥ śiśur iha vaktramaṇḍikārtaḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.16"><label>ut.27.16</label> yaḥ phenaṃ vamati vinamyate ca
                        madhye sodvegaṃ vilapati cordhvamīkṣamāṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jvaryeta pratatamatho vasāsagandhir niḥsaṃjño bhavati hi naigameṣajuṣṭaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.17"><label>ut.27.17</label> prastabdho yaḥ stanadveṣī muhyate
                        cāviśanmuhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         taṃ bālamacirāddhanti grahaḥ saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.18"><label>ut.27.18</label> viparītamataḥ sādhyaṃ
                        cikitsedacirārditam |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛhe purāṇahaviṣābhyajya bālaṃ śucau śuciḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.19"><label>ut.27.19</label> sarṣapān prakiretteṣāṃ
                        tailairdīpaṃ ca kārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadā sannihitaṃ cāpi juhuyāddhavyavāhanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.20"><label>ut.27.20</label>
                        sarvagandhauṣadhībījairgandhamālyairalaṅkṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         agnye kṛttikābhyaś ca svāhā svāheti saṃtatam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.27.21"><label>ut.27.21</label> namaḥ skandāya devāya
                        grahādhipataye namaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirasā tvābhivande 'haṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva me balim |
                        <caesura/>
                         nīrujo nirvikāraś ca śiśurme jāyatāṃ drutam ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
                        navagrahākṛtivijñānīyo nāma (prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        ||27 ||</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.28.9"><label>ut.28.9</label> snānaṃ trirātraṃ niśi catvareṣu

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.28.10"><label>ut.28.10</label> rakṣāmataḥ pravakṣyāmi bālānāṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.28.11"><label>ut.28.11</label> tapasāṃ tejasāṃ caiva yaśasāṃ

                <div n="29" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ekonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.29.1"><label>ut.29.1</label> athātaḥ skandāpasmārapratiṣedhaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.29.3"><label>ut.29.3</label> bilvaḥ śirīṣo golomī surasādiś ca

                         pariṣeke prayoktavyaḥ skandāpasmāraśāntaye || </l>

                        tailamabhyañjane hitam |

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.29.5ab"><label>ut.29.5</label> vipaktavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāpi pānīyaṃ
                        payasā saha |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.29.5cd"> utsādanaṃ vacāhiṅguyuktaṃ skandagrahe hitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.29.7"><label>ut.29.7</label> anantāṃ kukkuṭīṃ bimbīṃ markaṭīṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.29.8"><label>ut.29.8</label> bhūtaudano nivedyaś ca
                        skandāpasmāriṇe 'vaṭe |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.29.9"><label>ut.29.9</label> skandāpasmārasaṃjño yaḥ skandasya
                        dayitaḥ sakhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśākhasaṃjñaś ca śiśoḥ śivo 's tu vikṛtānanaḥ ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
