                <div n="30" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.1"><label>ut.30.1</label> athātaḥ śakunīpratīṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.2"><label>ut.30.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.3"><label>ut.30.3</label> śakunyabhiparītasya kāryo vaidyena
                        jānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vetasāmrakapitthānāṃ niṣkvāthaḥ pariṣecane || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.4ab"><label>ut.30.4</label> kaṣāyamadhurais tailaṃ
                        kāryamabhyañjane śiśoḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.4cd"> madhukośīrahrīberasārivotpalapadmakaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.5ab"><label>ut.30.5</label> rodhrapriyaṅgumañjiṣṭhāgairikaiḥ
                        pradihec chiśum |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.5cd"> vraṇeṣūktāni cūrṇāni pathyāni vividhāni ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.6ab"><label>ut.30.6</label> skandagrahe dhūpanāni tānīhāpi
                        prayojayet |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.6cd"> śatāvarīmṛgair vārunāgadantīnidigdhikāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.7ab"><label>ut.30.7</label> lakṣmaṇāṃ sahadevāṃ ca bṛhatīṃ
                        cāpi dhārayet |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.7cd"> tilataṇḍulakaṃ mālyaṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.8"><label>ut.30.8</label> balirepa karañjeṣu nivedyo
                        niyatātmanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣkuṭe ca prayoktavyaṃ snānamasya yathāvidhi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.9"><label>ut.30.9</label> skandāpasmāraśamanaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāpīha
                        pūjitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāc ca vividhāṃ pūjāṃ śakunyāḥ kusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.10"><label>ut.30.10</label> antarīkṣacarā devī
                        sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ayomukhī tīkṣṇatuṇḍā śakunī te prasīdatu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.30.11"><label>ut.30.11</label> durdarśanā mahākāyā piṅgākṣī
                        bhairavasvarā |
                        <caesura/>
                         lambodarī śaṅkukarṇī śakunī te prasīdatu ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
                        śakunīpratiṣedho nāma (caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || 30

                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāmarthe tataḥ skandaḥ śivaṃ devamacodayat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.13"><label>ut.37.13</label> tato grahāṃstānuvāca bhagavān
                        bhaganetrahṛt |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryagyoniṃ mānuṣaṃ ca tritayaṃ jagat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.14"><label>ut.37.14</label> parasparopakāreṇa vartate
                        dhāryate 'pi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         devā manuṣyān prīṇanti tairyagyonīṃs tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.15"><label>ut.37.15</label> vartamānairyathākālaṃ
                        śītavarṣoṣṇamārutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ijyāñjalinamaskārajapahomavratādibhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.16"><label>ut.37.16</label> narāḥ samyak prayuktaiś ca
                        prīṇanti tridiveśvarān |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhāgadheyaṃ vibhaktaṃ ca śeṣaṃ kiñcin na vidyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.17"><label>ut.37.17</label> tadyuṣmākaṃ śubhā vṛttirbāleṣveva
                        bhaviṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuleṣu yeṣu nejyante devāḥ pitara eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.18"><label>ut.37.18</label> brāhmaṇāḥ sādhavaś caiva guravo
                        'tithayas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivṛttācāraśauceṣu parapākopajīviṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.19"><label>ut.37.19</label> utsannabalibhikṣeṣu
                        bhinnakāṃsyopabhojiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛheṣu teṣu ye bālāstān gṛhṇīdhvamaśaṅkitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.20"><label>ut.37.20</label> tatra vo vipulā vṛttiḥ pūjā caiva
                        bhaviṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ grahāḥ samutpannā bālān gṛhṇanti cāpy ataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.21"><label>ut.37.21</label> grahopasṛṣṭā bālāstu duś
                        cikitsyatamā matāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaikalyaṃ maraṇaṃ cāpi dhruvaṃ skandagrahe matam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.37.22"><label>ut.37.22</label> skandagraho 'tyugratamaḥ sarveṣv
                        eva yataḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anyo vā sarvarūpas tu na sādhyo graha ucyate ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
                        grahotpattyadhyāyo nāma (ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) saptatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        ||37 ||</p>
                </div>

                        'tisārapratiṣedho nāma (dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ/) catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||40
                        ||</p>
                </div>

                         janayanti nṛṇāṃ gulmaṃ sa pañcavidha ucyate || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.4"><label>ut.42.4</label> hṛdbastyor antare granthiḥ saṃcārī
                        yadi vācalaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cayāpacayavān vṛttaḥ sa gulma iti kīrtitaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.5ab"><label>ut.42.5</label> pañca gulmāśrayā nṝṇāṃ pārśve

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.5cd"><ref rend="superscript footnote marker"

                        abhidhīyate |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.6cd">sa yasmād ātmani cayaṃ gacchaty apsv iva budbudaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.7"><label>ut.42.7</label> antaḥ sarati yasmāc ca na pākam
                        upayātyataḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.8"><label>ut.42.8</label> puruṣāṇāṃ tathā strīṇāṃ jñeyo

                         sadanaṃ madantā vahner āṭopo 'ntravikūjanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.9cd"> dveṣo 'nne vāyurūrdhvaṃ ca pūrvarūpeṣu gulminām || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.10"><label>ut.42.10</label> hṛtkukṣiśūlaṃ mukhakaṇṭhaśoṣo
                        vāyor nirodho viṣamāgnitā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         te te vikārāḥ pavanātmakāś ca bhavanti gulme 'nilasaṃbhave tu || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.11"><label>ut.42.11</label>
                        svedajvarāhāravidāhadāhāstṛṣṇāṅgarāgaḥ kaṭuvaktratā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittasya liṅgānyakhilāni yāni pittātmake tāni bhavanti gulme || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.12"><label>ut.42.12</label> staimityam anne 'ruciraṅgasādaś
                        chardiḥ praseko madhurāsyatā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphasya liṅgāni ca yāni tāni bhavanti gulme kaphasaṃbhave tu || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.13"><label>ut.42.13</label> sarvātmakaḥ sarvavikārayuktaḥ so
                        'sādhya uktaḥ kṣatajaṃ pravakṣye |
                        <caesura/>
                         navaprasūtāhitabhojanā yā yā cāmagarbhaṃ visṛjedṛtau<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> vā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.14"><label>ut.42.14</label> vāyur hi tasyāḥ parigṛhya raktaṃ
                        karoti gulmaṃ sarujaṃ sadāham |
                        <caesura/>
                         paittasya liṅgena samānaliṅgaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ cāpy aparaṃ nibodha || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.15"><label>ut.42.15</label> na spandate nodarameti vṛddhiṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.96"><label>ut.42.96</label> pippalyaḥ pippalīmūlaṃ saindhavaṃ
                        ceti cūrṇayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāni cūrṇāni payasā pibet kāmbalikena vā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.97"><label>ut.42.97</label> madhvāsavena cukreṇa
                        surāsauvīrakeṇa vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         athavaitāni(athacaitāni) cūrṇāni mātuluṅgarasena vā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.98"><label>ut.42.98</label> tathā badarayūṣeṇa bhāvitāni
                        punaḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāni hiṅgupragāḍhāni saha śarkarayā pibet || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.99"><label>ut.42.99</label> saha dāḍimasāreṇa vartiḥ kāryā
                        bhiṣagjitā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.100"><label>ut.42.100</label> guḍatailena vā līḍhā pītā

                        <caesura/>
                         bubhukṣāprabhave śūle laghu saṃtarpaṇaṃ hitam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.101"><label>ut.42.101</label> uṣṇaiḥ kṣīrairyavāgūbhiḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.102"><label>ut.42.102</label> susaṃskṛtāḥ pradeyāḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.42.104"><label>ut.42.104</label> sa sukhaṃ chardayitvā tu pītvā

                        gulmapratiṣedho nāma (caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||42

                <div n="44" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>catuś catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.1"><label>ut.44.1</label> athātaḥ pāṇḍurogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.2"><label>ut.44.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvandariḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.3"><label>ut.44.3</label> vyavāyamamlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ
                        divāsvapnamatīva tīkṣṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣevamāṇasya vidūṣya raktaṃ kurvanti doṣāstvaci pāṇḍubhāvam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.4"><label>ut.44.4</label> pāṇḍvāmayo 'ṣṭārdhavidhaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ
                        pṛthaksamastairyugapac ca doṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣu caiteṣv iha pāṇḍubhāvo yato 'dhiko 'taḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.5"><label>ut.44.5</label> tvaksphoṭanaṃ ṣṭhīvanagātrasādau
                        mṛdbhakṣaṇaṃ prekṣaṇakūṭaśothaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                         lihet tathā vāstukabījacūrṇaṃ kṣaudrānvitaṃ taṇḍulasāhvayaṃ vā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.32"><label>ut.45.32</label> lihyāc ca lājāñjanacūrṇamekamevaṃ
                        sitākṣaudrayutāṃ tugākhyām |
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣāṃ sitāṃ tiktakarohiṇīṃ ca himāmbunā vā madhukena yuktām || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.33ab"><label>ut.45.33</label> pathyāmahiṃsrāṃ rajanīṃ ghṛtaṃ
                        ca
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyāt tathā śoṇitapittarogī |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.33cd"> vāsākaṣāyotpalamṛtpriyaṅgurodhrāñjanāmbhoruhakeśarāṇi
                        || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.34"><label>ut.45.34</label> pītvā sitākṣaudrayutāni jahyāt

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.35"><label>ut.45.35</label> puṣpāṇi śigroś ca vicūrṇya leho

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.36cd"> mūlāni puṣpāṇi ca mātuluṅgyāḥ piṣṭvā

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.37"><label>ut.45.37</label> ghrāṇapravṛtte jalamāśu deyaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.38"><label>ut.45.38</label> śītopacāraṃ madhuraṃ ca kuryād

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.39"><label>ut.45.39</label> kṣīreṇa cāsthāpanam agryam uktaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.41"><label>ut.45.41</label> kṣīraudanaṃ bhuktam athānuvāsayed

                    <p xml:id="SS.6.45">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.21"><label>ut.47.21</label> jñeyāni tatra bhiṣajā suviniś

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.22"><label>ut.47.22</label> dveṣaḥ surān navikṛteṣu ca teṣu

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.24"><label>ut.47.24</label> teṣāṃ nivāraṇam idaṃhi

                        <caesura/>

                            rend="superscript        footnote marker">1</ref> pavanasya śāntyai || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.25"><label>ut.47.25</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.26"><label>ut.47.26</label> seveta vā phalarasopahitān

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.27"><label>ut.47.27</label> pītvā ca madyam api
                        cekṣurasapragāḍhaṃ niḥśeṣataḥ kṣaṇamavasthitamullikhec ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         lāvaiṇatittirirasāṃś ca pibedanamlān maudgān sukhāya saghṛtān sasitāṃś ca
                        yūṣān || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.28"><label>ut.47.28</label> pānātyaye kaphakṛte
                        kaphamullikhec ca madyena bimbividulodakasaṃyutena |
                        <caesura/>
                         seveta tiktakaṭukāṃś ca rasānudārān yūṣāṃś ca tiktakaṭukopahitān hitāya || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.47.29"><label>ut.47.29</label> pathyaṃ yavānnavikṛtāni ca
                        jāṅgalāni śleṣmaghnamanyadapi yac ca niratyayaṃ syāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāc ca sarvamatha sarvabhave vidhānaṃ ddvandvodbhave dvayamavekṣya
                        yathāpradhānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.6"><label>ut.48.6</label> tisraḥ smṛtāstāḥ kṣatajā caturthī

                            marker">1</ref> liṅgānyanupūrvaśastu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.13"><label>ut.48.13</label> rasakṣayādyā kṣayajā matā sā

                        <caesura/>
                         atyarthamākāṅkṣati cāpi toyaṃ tāṃ sannipātāditi kecidāhuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.14"><label>ut.48.14</label> rasakṣayoktāni ca lakṣaṇāni
                        tasyāmaśeṣeṇa bhiṣagvyavasyet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tridoṣaliṅgāmasamudbhavā ca hṛcchūlaniṣṭhīvanasādayuktā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.15"><label>ut.48.15</label> snigdhaṃ tathāmlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca
                        bhuktaṃ gurvannamevātitṛṣāṃ karoti |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaṃ vicittaṃ badhiraṃ tṛṣārtaṃ vivarjayennirgatajihvamāśu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.16"><label>ut.48.16</label> tṛṣṇābhivṛddhāvudare ca pūrṇe taṃ
                        vāmayenmāgadhikodakena |
                        <caesura/>
                         vilobhanaṃ cātra hitaṃ vidheyaṃ syāddāḍimāmrātakamātuluṅgaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.17"><label>ut.48.17</label> tisraḥ prayogairiha sannivāryāḥ
                        śītaiś ca samyag rasavīryajātaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gaṇḍūṣamamlairvirase ca vaktre kuryāc chubhairāmalakasya cūrṇaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.18"><label>ut.48.18</label> suvarṇarūpyādibhir
                        agnitaptairloṣṭaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā sikatādibhir vā<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         jalaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ śamayet tu tṛṣṇāṃ saśarkaraṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ himaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.19"><label>ut.48.19</label> pañcāṅgikāḥ pañcagaṇā ya
                        uktāsteṣv ambu siddhaṃ prathame gaṇe vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ manujo<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>+acireṇa tṛṣo vimucyeta hi vātajāyāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.20"><label>ut.48.20</label> pittaghnavargais tu kṛtaḥ kaṣāyaḥ
                        saśarkaraḥ kṣaudrayutaḥ suśītaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītastṛṣāṃ pittakṛtāṃ nihanti kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ vāpyatha jīvanīyaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.21"><label>ut.48.21</label>
                            bilvāḍhakīkanyakapañcamūlīdarbheṣu<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> siddhaṃ kaphajāṃ nihanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaṃ bhavec chardanam eva cātra taptena nimbaprasavodakena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.22"><label>ut.48.22</label> sarvāsu tṛṣṇāsvathavāpi paittaṃ
                        kuryād vidhiṃ tena hi tā na santi |
                        <caesura/>
                         paryāgatodumbarajo rasas tu saśarkaratatkvathitodakaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.23"><label>ut.48.23</label> vargasya siddhasya ca sārivādeḥ
                        pātavyamambhaḥ śiśiraṃ tṛṣārtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaśeruśṛṅgāṭakapadmamocabisekṣusiddhaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> kṣatajāṃ nihanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.24"><label>ut.48.24</label> lājotpalośīrakucandanāni dattvā
                        pravāte niśi vāsayet tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         taduttamaṃ toyamudāragandhi sitāyutaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>vadanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.25"><label>ut.48.25</label> drākṣāpragāḍhaṃ ca hitāya vaidyas
                        tṛṣṇārditebhyo vitaren narebhyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sasārivādau tṛṇapañcamūle tathotpalādau <ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref>prathame gaṇe ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.26"><label>ut.48.26</label> kuryāt kaṣāyaṃ ca yatheritena<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> madhūkapuṣpādiṣu cāpareṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         rājādanakṣīrikapītaneṣu ṣaṭ pānakānyatra hitāni ca syuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.27"><label>ut.48.27</label> satuṇḍikerāṇyathavā pibettu
                        piṣṭāni kārpāsasamudbhavāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣatodbhavāṃ rugvinivāraṇena jayed rasānāmasṛjaś ca pānaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.28"><label>ut.48.28</label> kṣayotthitāṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ
                        nihanyānmāṃsodakaṃ vā madhukodakaṃ vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmodbhavāṃ bilvavacāyutais tu jayet kaṣāyairatha <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>dīpanīyaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.29"><label>ut.48.29</label> āmrātabhallātabalāyutāni pibet
                        kaṣāyāṇyatha dīpanāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurvannajātāṃ vamanairjayec ca kṣayādṛte sarvakṛtāṃ ca tṛṣṇām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.30"><label>ut.48.30</label> śramodbhavāṃ māṃsaraso nihanti
                        guḍodakaṃ vāpyathavāpi manthaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhaktoparodhāttṛṣito yavāgūmuṣṇāṃ piben manthamatho himaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.31"><label>ut.48.31</label> yā snehapītasya bhavec ca tṛṣṇā
                        tatroṣṇamambhaḥ prapiben manuṣyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madyodbhavāmardhajalaṃ nihanti madyaṃ tṛṣāṃ yāpi ca madyapasya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.32"><label>ut.48.32</label> tṛṣṇodbhavāṃ hanti jalaṃ suśītaṃ
                        saśarkaraṃ sekṣurasaṃ tathāmbhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svaiḥ svaiḥ kaṣāyairvamanāni tāsāṃ tathā jvaroktāni ca pācanāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.33"><label>ut.48.33</label> lepāvagāhau pariṣecanāni kuryāt
                        tathā śītagṛhāṇi cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśodhanaṃ kṣīrarasau ghṛtāni sarvāsu lehānmadhurān himāṃś ca ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
                        (daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ āditaḥ) aṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||48 ||</p>

                    <head>pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.1"><label>ut.50.1</label> athāto hikkāpratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.2"><label>ut.50.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.3"><label>ut.50.3</label> vidāhiguruviṣṭambhir
                        ūkṣābhiṣyandibhojanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītapānāsanasthānarajodhūmānilānalaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.4"><label>ut.50.4</label>
                        vyāyāmakarmabhārādhvavegāghātāpatarpaṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmadoṣābhighātastrīkṣayadoṣaprapīḍanaiḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.5"><label>ut.50.5</label> viṣamāśanādhyanaśanais tathā
                        samaśanair api |
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkā śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca nṛṇāṃ samupajāyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.6"><label>ut.50.6</label> muhurmuhurvāyurudeti sasvano
                        yakṛtplihāntrāṇi mukhādivākṣipan |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa ghoṣavānāśu hinastyasūn yatastatas tu hikketi bhiṣagbhir ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.7"><label>ut.50.7</label> annajāṃ yamalāṃ kṣudrāṃ gambhīrāṃ
                        mahatīṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāyuḥ kaphenānugataḥ pañca hikkāḥ karoti hi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.8"><label>ut.50.8</label> mukhaṃ kaṣāyamaratirgauravaṃ
                        kaṇṭhavakṣasoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvarūpāṇi hikkānāmāṭopo jaṭharasya ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.9"><label>ut.50.9</label> tvaramāṇasya cāhāraṃ
                        bhuñjānasyāthavā ghanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāyurannairavastīrṇaḥ kaṭukairardito bhṛśam<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.10"><label>ut.50.10</label> hikkayatyūrdhvago bhūtvā tāṃ
                        vidyādannajāṃ bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         cireṇa yamalairvegairyā hikkā saṃpravartate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.11"><label>ut.50.11</label> kampayantī śirogrīvaṃ yamalāṃ tāṃ
                        vinirdiśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikṛṣṭakālairyā vegairmandaiḥ samabhivartate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.12"><label>ut.50.12</label> kṣudrikā nāma sā hikkā jatrumūlāt
                        pradhāvitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nābhipravṛttā yā hikkā ghorā gambhīranādinī || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.13"><label>ut.50.13</label>
                        śuṣkauṣṭhakaṇṭhajihvāsyaśvāsapārśvarujākarī |
                        <caesura/>
                         anekopadravayutā gambhīrā nāma sā smṛtā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.14"><label>ut.50.14</label> marmāṇyāpīḍayantīva satataṃ yā
                        pravartate |
                        <caesura/>
                         dehamāyamya vegena ghoṣayatyatitṛṣyataḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahāhikketi sā jñeyā sarvagātraprakampinī || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.15"><label>ut.50.15</label> āyamyate hikkato 'ṅgāni yasya
                        dṛṣṭiś cordhvaṃ tāmyate yasya gāḍham |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇo 'nnadviṭ kāsate yaś ca hikkī tau dvāvantyau varjayed dhikkamānau || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.16"><label>ut.50.16</label> prāṇāyāmodvejanatrāsanāni
                        sūcītodaiḥ saṃbhramaś cātra śastaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭyāhvaṃ vā mākṣikeṇāvapīḍe pippalyo vā śarkarācūrṇayuktāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.17"><label>ut.50.17</label> sarpiḥ koṣṇaṃ kṣīramikṣo raso vā
                        nātikṣīṇe chardanaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>śāntihetoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nārīpayaḥpiṣṭamaśuklacandanaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca sasaindhavaṃ tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.18"><label>ut.50.18</label> cūrṇīkṛtaṃ saindhavamambhasāthavā
                        nihanti hikkāṃ ca hitaṃ ca nasyataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuñjyāddhūmaṃ śālaniryāsajātaṃ naipālaṃ vā goviṣāṇodbhavaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.19"><label>ut.50.19</label> sarpiḥsnigdhaiś carmabālaiḥ kṛtaṃ
                        vā hikkāsthāne svedanaṃ cāpi kāryam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudropetaṃ gairikaṃ kāñcanāhvaṃ lihyādbhasma grāmyasattvāsthijaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.20"><label>ut.50.20</label>
                        tadvacchvāvinmeṣagośalyakānāṃ(gośallakānāṃ) romāṇyantardhūmadagdhāni cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhvājyāktaṃ barhipatraprasūtamevaṃ bhasmaudumbaraṃ tailvakaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.21"><label>ut.50.21</label> svarjikṣāraṃ bījapūrādrasena
                        kṣaudropetaṃ hanti līḍhvāśu hikkām |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥsnigdhā ghnanti hikkāṃ yavāgvaḥ koṣṇagrāsāḥ pāyaso vā sukhoṣṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.22"><label>ut.50.22</label> śuṇṭhītoye sādhitaṃ kṣīramājaṃ
                        tadvat pītaṃ śarkarāsaṃyutaṃ vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ātṛptervā sevyamānaṃ nihantyād ghrātaṃ hikkāmāśu mūtraṃ tvajāvyoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.23"><label>ut.50.23</label> sapūtikīṭaṃ
                            laśunogragandhāhiṅgvabjamācūrṇya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> subhāvitaṃ tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudraṃ sitāṃ vāraṇakeśaraṃ ca pibedrasenekṣumadhūkajena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.24"><label>ut.50.24</label> pibet palaṃ vā lavaṇottamasya
                        dvābhyāṃ palābhyāṃ haviṣaḥ samagram |
                        <caesura/>
                         harītakīṃ koṣṇajalānupānāṃ pibed ghṛtaṃ kṣāramadhūpapannam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.25"><label>ut.50.25</label> rasaṃ kapitthānmadhupippalībhyāṃ
                        śuktipramāṇaṃ prapibet sukhāya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.26"><label>ut.50.26</label> kṛṣṇāṃ sitāṃ cāmalakaṃ ca līḍhaṃ
                        saśṛṅgaveraṃ madhunāthavāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         kolāsthimajjāñjanalājacūrṇaṃ hikkā nihanyānmadhunāvalīḍham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.27"><label>ut.50.27</label> pāṭalāyāḥ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ gairikaṃ
                        kaṭurohiṇī |
                        <caesura/>
                         kharjūramadhyaṃ māgadhyaḥ kāśīśaṃ dadhināma ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.28"><label>ut.50.28</label> catvāra ete yogāḥ syuḥ
                        pratipādapradarśitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhudvitīyāḥ kartavyāste hikkāsu vijānatā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.29"><label>ut.50.29</label>
                        kapotapārāvatalāvaśaka(lla)śvadaṃṣṭragodhāvṛṣadaṃśajān rasān |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet phalāmlānahimān sasaindhavān snigdhāṃstathaivarṣyamṛgadvijodbhavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.50.30"><label>ut.50.30</label> virecanaṃ pathyatamaṃ
                        sasaindhavaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca sitopalāyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadāgatāvūrdhvagate 'nuvāsanaṃ vadanti kecic ca hitāya hikkinām ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
                        hikkāpratiṣedho nāma (dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||50
                        ||</p>

                        <caesura/>

                        hiṅgvardhayuktāṃ madhunā suyuktām |
                        <caesura/>

                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>pavanānuviddho vajraṃ yathā vā
                        surarājamuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogāstathaite khalu durnivārāḥ śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca vilambikā ca ||</l>

                <div n="52" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.1"><label>ut.52.1</label> athātaḥ kāsapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.2"><label>ut.52.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.3"><label>ut.52.3</label> uktā ye hetavo nṝṇāṃ rogayoḥ
                        śvāsahikkayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsasyāpi ca vijñeyāsta evotpattihetavaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.4"><label>ut.52.4</label> dhūmopaghātādrajasastathaiva
                        vyāyāmarūkṣānnaniṣevaṇāc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vimārgagatvād api bhojanasya vegāvarodhāt kṣavathos tathaiva || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.5"><label>ut.52.5</label> prāṇo hyudānānugataḥ praduṣṭaḥ
                        saṃbhinnakāṃsyasvanatulyaghoṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nireti vaktrāt sahasā sadoṣaḥ kāsaḥ sa vidvadbhir udāhṛtas tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.6"><label>ut.52.6</label> sa vātapittaprabhavaḥ kaphāc ca
                        kṣatāttathānyaḥ kṣayajo 'paraś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcaprakāraḥ kathito bhiṣagbhir vivardhito yakṣmavikārakṛt syāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.7"><label>ut.52.7</label> bhaviṣyatas tasya tu
                        kaṇṭhakaṇḍūrbhojyoparodho galatālulepaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svaśabdavaiṣamyamarocako 'gnisādaś ca liṅgāni bhavantyamūni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.8"><label>ut.52.8</label> hṛcchaṅkhamūrdhodarapārśvaśūlī
                        kṣāmānanaḥ kṣīṇabalasvaraujāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasaktamantaḥkaphamīraṇena kāset tu śuṣkaṃ svarabhedayuktaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.9"><label>ut.52.9</label>
                        urovidāhajvaravaktraśoṣairabhyarditastiktamukhastṛṣārtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittena pītāni vamet kaṭūni kāset sa pāṇḍuḥ paridahyamānaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.10"><label>ut.52.10</label> pralipyamānena(vilipyamānena)
                        mukhena sīdan śirorujārtaḥ kaphapūrṇadehaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhaktaruggauravasādayuktaḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>kāseta nā sāndrakaphaṃ kaphena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.11"><label>ut.52.11</label> vakṣo 'timātraṃ vihataṃ tu yasya
                        vyāyāmabhārādhyayanābhighātaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśliṣṭavakṣāḥ sa naraḥ saraktaṃ ṣṭhīvatyabhīkṣṇaṃ kṣatajaṃ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> tamūhuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.12"><label>ut.52.12</label> sa gātraśūlajvaradāhamohān
                        prāṇakṣayaṃ copalabheta kāsī |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuṣyan viniṣṭhīvati durbalas tu prakṣīṇamāṃso rudhiraṃ sapūyam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.13"><label>ut.52.13</label> sasarvaliṅgaṃ bhṛśaduś cikitsyaṃ
                        cikitsitajñāḥ kṣayajaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>vadanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         vṛddhatvamāsādya bhavet tu yo vai yāpyaṃ tamāhurbhiṣajas tu kāsam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.14"><label>ut.52.14</label>
                        śṛṅgīvacākaṭphalakattṛṇābdadhānyābhayābhārgyamarāhvaviśvam |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇāmbunā hiṅguyutaṃ tu pītvā baddhāsyamapyāśu jahāti kāsam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.15"><label>ut.52.15</label>
                            phalatrikavyoṣaviḍaṅgaśṛṅgīrāsnāvacāpadmakadevakāṣṭhaiḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         lehaḥ samaiḥ kṣaudrasitāghṛtāktaḥ kāsaṃ nihanyādacirādudīrṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.16"><label>ut.52.16</label> pathyāṃ sitāmāmalakāni lājāṃ
                        samāgadhīṃ cāpi vicūrṇya śuṇṭhīm |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpirmadhubhyāṃ vilihīta kāsī sasaindhavāṃ voṣṇajalena kṛṣṇām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.17"><label>ut.52.17</label> khādedguḍaṃ nāgarapippalībhyāṃ
                        drākṣāṃ ca sarpirmadhunāvalihyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣāṃ sitāṃ māgadhikāṃ ca tulyāṃ saśṛṅgaveraṃ madhukaṃ tugāṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.18"><label>ut.52.18</label> lihyād ghṛtakṣaudrayutāṃ samāṃśāṃ
                        sitopalāṃ vā maricāṃśayuktām |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhātrīkaṇāviśvasitopalāś ca saṃcūrṇya maṇḍena pibec ca dadhnaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.19"><label>ut.52.19</label> hareṇukāṃ māgadhikāṃ ca <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>tulyāṃ dadhnā pibet
                        kāsagadābhibhūtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ubhe haridre suradāruśuṇṭhīṃ gāyatrisāraṃ ca pibet samāṃśam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.20"><label>ut.52.20</label> bastasya mūtreṇa sukhāmbunā vā
                        dantīṃ dravantīṃ ca satilvakākhyām<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhṛṣṭāni sarpīṃṣyatha bādarāṇi khādet palāśāni sasaindhavāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.21"><label>ut.52.21</label> kolapramāṇaṃ prapibeddhi hiṅgu
                        sauvīrakeṇāmlarasena vāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudreṇa lihyānmaricāni vāpi bhārgīvacāhiṅgukṛtā ca vartiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.22"><label>ut.52.22</label> dhūme praśastā ghṛtasaṃprayuktā
                        veṇutvagelālavaṇaiḥ kṛtā vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         musteṅgudītvaṅmadhukāhvamāṃsīmanaḥśilālaiś chagalāmbupiṣṭaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.23"><label>ut.52.23</label> vidhāya vartīś ca payo 'nupānaṃ
                        dhūmaṃ pibedvātabalāsakāsī |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibec ca sīdhuṃ maricānvitaṃ vā tenāśu kāsaṃ jayati prasahya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.24"><label>ut.52.24</label> drākṣāmbumañjiṣṭhapurāhvayābhiḥ
                        kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ mākṣikasaṃprayuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         nidigdhikānāgarapippalībhiḥ khādec ca mudgānmadhunā susiddhān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.25"><label>ut.52.25</label> utkārikāṃ sarpiṣi nāgarāḍhyāṃ
                        paktvā samūlaistruṭikolapatraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ebhir niṣeveta kṛtāṃ ca peyāṃ tanvīṃ suśītāṃ madhunā vimiśrām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.26"><label>ut.52.26</label> yat plīhni sarpirvihitaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ
                        tadvātakāsaṃ jayati prasahya |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārigandhādikṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā rasena vā vāsakajena pakvam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.27"><label>ut.52.27</label> virecanaṃ snaihikamatra
                        coktamāsthāpanaṃ cāpy anuvāsanaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmaṃ pibet snaihikamapramattaḥ pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ ghṛtam eva cātra || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.28"><label>ut.52.28</label> hitā yavāgvaś ca raseṣu siddhāḥ
                        payāṃsi lehāḥ saghṛtās tathaiva |
                        <caesura/>
                         pracchardanaṃ kāyaśirovirekās tathaiva dhūmāḥ kavalagrahāś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.29"><label>ut.52.29</label> uṣṇāś ca lehāḥ kaṭukā nihanyuḥ
                        kaphaṃ viśeṣeṇa viśoṣaṇaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭutrikaṃ cāpi vadanti pathyaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṛmighnasvarase vipakvam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.30"><label>ut.52.30</label> nirguṇḍipatrasvarase ca pakvaṃ
                        sarpiḥ kaphotthaṃ vinihanti kāsam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṭhāviḍavyoṣaviḍaṅgasindhutrikaṇṭarāsnāhutabhugbalābhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.31"><label>ut.52.31</label>
                        śṛṅgīvacāmbhodharadevadārudurālabhābhārgyabhayaśaṭībhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag vipakvaṃ dviguṇena sarpirnidigdhikāyāḥ svarasena caitat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.32"><label>ut.52.32</label>
                            śvāsāgnisādasvarabhedabhinnānnihantyudīrṇānapi<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> pañca kāsān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārigandhotpalasārivādīn niṣkvāthya <ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref>vargaṃ madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.33"><label>ut.52.33</label> ghṛtaṃ pacedikṣurasāmbudugdhaiḥ
                        kākolivarge ca saśarkaraṃ tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         prātaḥ pibet pittakṛte ca kāse ratiprasūte kṣataje ca kāse || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.34"><label>ut.52.34</label>
                        kharjūrabhārgīmagadhāpriyālamadhūlikailāmalakaiḥ samāṃśaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇaṃ sitākṣaudraghṛtaprāgāḍhaṃ trīn hanti kāsānupayujyamānam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.35"><label>ut.52.35</label>
                        raktāharidrāñjanavahnipāṭhāmūrvopakulyā vilihet samāṃśāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudreṇa kāse kṣataje kṣayotthe pibed ghṛtaṃ cekṣurase vipakvam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.36"><label>ut.52.36</label> cūrṇaṃ pibed āmalakasya vāpi
                        kṣīreṇa pakvaṃ saghṛtaṃ hitāśī |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇāni godhūmayavodbhavāni kākolivargaś ca kṛtaḥ susūkṣmaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.37"><label>ut.52.37</label> kāseṣu peyastriṣu kāsavadbhiḥ
                        kṣīreṇa sakṣaudraghṛtena vāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         guḍodakaṃ vā kvathitaṃ pibeddhi kṣaudreṇa śītaṃ maricopadaṃśam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.38"><label>ut.52.38</label> prasthatrayeṇāmalakīrasasya
                        śuddhasya dattvārdhatulāṃ guḍasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇīkṛtairgranthikacavyajīravyoṣebhakṛṣṇāhapuṣājamodaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.39"><label>ut.52.39</label>
                        viḍaṅgasindhutriphalāyavānīpāṭhāgnidhānyaiś ca picupramāṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dattvā trivṛccūrṇapalāni cāṣṭāvaṣṭau ca tailasya pacedyathāvat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.40"><label>ut.52.40</label> taṃ bhakṣayed akṣaphalapramāṇaṃ
                        yatheṣṭaceṣṭastrisugandhiyuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         anena sarve grahaṇīvikārāḥ saśvāsakāsasvarabhedaśothāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.41"><label>ut.52.41</label> śāmyanti cāyaṃ
                        ciramantaragnerhatasya puṃstvasya ca vṛddhihetuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         strīṇāṃ ca vandhyāmayanāśanaḥ syāt kalyāṇako nāma guḍaḥ pratītaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.42"><label>ut.52.42</label>
                        dvipañcamūlebhakaṇātmaguptābhārgīśaṭīpuṣkaramūlaviśvān |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṭhāmṛtāgranthikaśaṅkhapuṣpīrāsnāgnyapāmārgabalāyavāsān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.43"><label>ut.52.43</label> dvipālikān <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>nyasya yavāḍhakaṃ ca harītakīnāṃ ca śataṃ
                        gurūṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         droṇe jalasyāḍhakasaṃyute ca kvāthe kṛte pūtacaturthabhāge || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.44"><label>ut.52.44</label> pacettulāṃ śuddhaguḍasya dattvā
                        pṛthak ca tailāt kuḍavaṃ ghṛtāc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇaṃ ca tāvan magadhodbhavāyā deyaṃ ca tasmin madhu siddhaśīte || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.45"><label>ut.52.45</label> rasāyanāt karṣamato vilihyāddve
                        cābhaye nityam athāśu hanyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad rājayakṣmagrahaṇīpradoṣaśophāgnimāndyasvarabhedakāsān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.46"><label>ut.52.46</label> pāṇḍvāmayaśvāsaśirovikārān
                        hṛdrogahikkāviṣam ajvarāṃś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         medhābalotsāham atipradaṃ ca cakāra caitad bhagavān agastyaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.52.47"><label>ut.52.47</label>
                        kulīraśuktīcaṭakaiṇalāvānniṣkvāthya vargaṃ madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pacedghṛtaṃ tat tu niṣevyamāṇaṃ hanyāt kṣatotthaṃ kṣayajaṃ ca kāsam ||
                        śatāvarīnāgabalāvipakvaṃ ghṛtaṃ vidheyaṃ ca hitāya kāsinām | </l>

                    <l/>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
                        kāsapratiṣedho nāma (caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        ||52 ||</p>
                </div>



                <div n="53" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.1"><label>ut.53.1</label> athātaḥ
                        svarabhedapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.2"><label>ut.53.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.3"><label>ut.53.3</label> atyuc
                            cabhāṣaṇaviṣādhyayanātigītaśītādibhiḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> prakupitāḥ pavanādayas tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotaḥsu te svaravaheṣu gatāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ hanyuḥ svaraṃ bhavati cāpi hi
                        ṣaḍvidhaḥ saḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.4"><label>ut.53.4</label> vātena kṛṣṇanayanānanamūtravarcā
                        bhinnaṃ śanair vadati gadgadavat svaraṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittena pītavadanākṣipurīṣamūtro brūyād galena <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>paridāhasamanvitena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.5"><label>ut.53.5</label> kṛcchrāt kaphena satataṃ
                        kapharuddhakaṇṭho mandaṃ śanairvadati cāpi divā viśeṣaḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvātmake bhavati sarvavikārasaṃpadavyaktatā ca vacasastamasādhyam āhuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.6"><label>ut.53.6</label> dhūpyeta vāk kṣayakṛte
                        kṣayamāpnuyāc ca vāgeṣa cāpi(vāpi) hatavāk parivarjanīyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         antargalaṃ svaramalakṣyapadaṃ cireṇa <ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref>medaś cayādvadati digdhagalauṣṭhatāluḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.7"><label>ut.53.7</label> kṣīṇasya vṛddhasya kṛśasya cāpi
                        cirotthito yaś ca sahopajātaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         medasvinaḥ sarvasamudbhavaś ca svarāmayo yo na sa siddhimeti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.8"><label>ut.53.8</label> snigdhān
                        svarāturanarānapakṛṣṭadoṣān nyāyena <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref>tān vamanarecanabastibhiś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyāvapīḍamukhadhāvanadhūmalehaiḥ saṃpādayec ca vividhaiḥ kavalagrahaiś ca
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.9"><label>ut.53.9</label> yaḥ śvāsakāsavidhirādita eva
                        coktastaṃ cāpy aśeṣamavatārayituṃ yateta |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaiśeṣikaṃ ca vidhimūrdhvamato vadāmi taṃ vai svarāturahitaṃ nikhilaṃ
                        nibodha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.10"><label>ut.53.10</label> svaropaghāte 'nilaje bhuktopari
                        ghṛtaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsamardakavātārkamārkavasvarase śṛtam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.11"><label>ut.53.11</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ hantyanilaṃ
                        siddhamārtagale rase |
                        <caesura/>
                         yavakṣārājamodābhyāṃ citrakāmalakeṣu vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.12"><label>ut.53.12</label> devadārvagnikābhyāṃ vā
                        siddhāmājaṃ samākṣikam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhodakānupāno vā sasarpiṣko guḍaudanaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.13"><label>ut.53.13</label> kṣīrānupānaṃ pitte tu pibet
                        sarpiratandritaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśnīyāc ca sasarpiṣkaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukapāyasam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.14"><label>ut.53.14</label> lihyānmadhurakāṇāṃ vā cūrṇaṃ
                        madhughṛtāplutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvarīcūrṇayogaṃ balācūrṇam athāpi vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.15"><label>ut.53.15</label> pibet kaṭūni mūtreṇa kaphaje
                        svarasaṃkṣaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyādvā madhutailābhyāṃ bhuktvā khādet kaṭūni vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.16"><label>ut.53.16</label> svaropaghāte medoje
                        kaphavadvidhiriṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvaje kṣayaje cāpi pratyākhyāyācaret kriyām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.53.17"><label>ut.53.17</label> śarkarāmadhumiśrāṇi śṛtāni
                        madhuraiḥ saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet payāṃsi yasyoc cairvadato 'bhihataḥ svaraḥ ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
                        chardipratiṣedho nāma (pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        ||53 ||</p>
                </div>
                <div n="54" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>catuḥpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.1"><label>ut.54.1</label> athātaḥ kṛmirogapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.2"><label>ut.54.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.3"><label>ut.54.3</label>
                        ajīrṇādhyaśanāsātmyaviruddhamalināśanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avyāyāmadivāsvapnagurvatisnigdhaśītalaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.4"><label>ut.54.4</label>
                        māṣapiṣṭānnavidalabisaśālūkaserukaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         parṇaśākasurāśuktad adhikṣīraguḍekṣubhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.5"><label>ut.54.5</label>
                        palalānūpapiśitapiṇyākapṛthukādibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svādvamladravapānaiś ca śleṣmā pittaṃ ca kupyati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.6"><label>ut.54.6</label> kṛmīn bahuvidhākārān karoti
                        vividhāśrayān |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmapakvāśaye teṣāṃ kaphaviḍjanmanāṃ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhamanyāṃ raktajānāṃ ca prasavaḥ prāyaśaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.7"><label>ut.54.7</label> viṃśateḥ kṛmijātīnāṃ trividhaḥ
                        saṃbhavaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         purīṣakapharaktāni tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vistaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.8"><label>ut.54.8</label> ajavā vijavāḥ<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> kipyāś cipyā gaṇḍūpadās tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūravo dvimukhāś caiva jñeyāḥ sapta purīṣajāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.9"><label>ut.54.9</label> śvetāḥ sūkṣmāstudantyete gudaṃ
                        pratisaranti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāmevāpare pucchaiḥ pṛthavaś ca bhavanti hi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.10"><label>ut.54.10</label>
                        śūlāgnimāndyapāṇḍutvaviṣṭambhabalasaṃkṣayāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasekārucihṛdrogaviḍbhedās tu purīṣajaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.11"><label>ut.54.11</label> raktā gaṇḍūpadā dīrghā
                        gudakaṇḍūnipātinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śūlāṭopaśakṛdbhedapaktināśakarāś ca te || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.12"><label>ut.54.12</label> darbhapuṣpā mahāpuṣpāḥ pralūnāś

                        <caesura/>
                         pipīlikā dāruṇāś ca kaphakopasamudbhavāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.13"><label>ut.54.13</label> romaśā romamūrdhānaḥ sapucchāḥ

                        <caesura/>
                         rūḍhadhānyāṅkurākārāḥ śuklāste tanavas tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.14"><label>ut.54.14</label> majjādā
                        netraleḍhārastāluśrotrabhujas tathā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.15"><label>ut.54.15</label> keśaromanakhādāś ca dantādāḥ
                        kikkiśās tathā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.16"><label>ut.54.16</label> te saraktāś ca kṛṣṇāś ca snigdhāś

                         raktādhiṣṭhānajān prāyo vikārān janayanti te || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.17"><label>ut.54.17</label> māṣapiṣṭānnavidalaparṇaśākaiḥ

                         māṃsamāṣaguḍakṣīradadhitailaiḥ kaphodbhavāḥ || </l>

                        <caesura/>
                         jvaro vivarṇatā śūlaṃ hṛdrogaḥ sadanaṃ bhramaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.19"><label>ut.54.19</label> bhaktadveṣo 'tisāraś ca

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.20"><label>ut.54.20</label> keśādādyāstvadṛśyāste dvāvādyau

                        <caesura/>

                        surasādergaṇasya ca |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.23"><label>ut.54.23</label> pratyāgate nirūhe tu naraṃ snātaṃ
                        sukhāmbunā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.24"><label>ut.54.24</label> snehenoktena cainaṃ tu yojayet
                        snehabastinā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.25"><label>ut.54.25</label> kevūkasvarasaṃ vāpi
                        pūrvavattīkṣṇabhojanaḥ |

                        svarasaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pattūrasvarasaṃ vāpi pibedvā surasādijam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.27"><label>ut.54.27</label> lihyādaśvaśakṛccūrṇaṃ vaiḍaṅgaṃ

                        vā dadhimastunā |
                        <caesura/>
                         purīṣajān kaphotthāṃś ca hanyādevaṃ kṛmīn bhiṣak || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.34"><label>ut.54.34</label> śirohṛdghrāṇakarṇākṣisaṃśritāṃś

                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣeṇāñjanairnasyairavapīḍaiś ca sādhayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.35"><label>ut.54.35</label> śakṛdrasaṃ turaṅgasya suśuṣkaṃ
                        bhāvayed ati |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣkvāthena viḍaṅgānāṃ cūrṇaṃ pradhamanaṃ tu tat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.36"><label>ut.54.36</label> ayaś cūrṇānyanenaiva vidhinā

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.38"><label>ut.54.38</label> raktajānāṃ pratīkāraṃ kuryāt

                            marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.40"><label>ut.54.40</label> kṣīrāṇi māṃsāni ghṛtāni caiva

                        <caesura/>
                         samāsato 'mlānmadhurān himāṃś ca kṛmīn jighāṃsuḥ parivarjayet tu ||</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         srotāṃsyudāvartayati purīṣaṃ cātivartayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.39"><label>ut.55.39</label> tato hṛdbastiśūlārto
                        gauravārucipīḍitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi kṛcchreṇa kurute naraḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.40"><label>ut.55.40</label>
                        śvāsakāsapratiśyāyadāhamohavamijvarān |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇāhikkāśirorogamanaḥśravaṇavibhramān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.41"><label>ut.55.41</label> labhate ca bahūnanyān vikārān
                        vātakopajān |
                        <caesura/>
                         taṃ tailalavaṇābhyaktaṃ snigdhaṃ svinnaṃ nirūhayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.42"><label>ut.55.42</label> doṣato bhinnavarcaskaṃ bhuktaṃ
                        cāpy anuvāsayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cec chāntiṃ vrajatyevamudāvartaḥ sudāruṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.43"><label>ut.55.43</label> athainaṃ bahuśaḥ svinnaṃ yuñjyāt
                        snehavirecanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāyayeta trivṛtpīluyavānīramlapācanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.44"><label>ut.55.44</label> hiṅgukuṣṭhavacāsvarjiviḍaṅgaṃ vā
                        dviruttaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         yogāvetāvudāvartaṃ śūlaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>cānilajaṃ hataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.45"><label>ut.55.45</label> devadārvagnikau kuṣṭhaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>śuṇṭhīṃ pathyāṃ palaṅkaṣām |
                        <caesura/>
                         pauṣkarāṇi ca mūlāni toyasyardhāḍhake pacet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.46"><label>ut.55.46</label> pādāvaśiṣṭaṃ tat
                        pītamudāvartamapohati |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūlakaṃ śuṣkamārdraṃ ca varṣābhūḥ pañcamūlakam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.47"><label>ut.55.47</label> ārevataphalaṃ cāpsu paktvā tena
                        ghṛtaṃ pacet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tat pīyamānaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>śāstyugramudāvartamaśeṣataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.48"><label>ut.55.48</label> vacāmativiṣāṃ kuṣṭhaṃ yavakṣāraṃ
                        harītakīm |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇāṃ nirdahanīṃ cāpi pibeduṣṇena vāriṇā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.49"><label>ut.55.49</label> ikṣvākumūlaṃ madanaṃ
                        viśalyātiviṣe vacām |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuṣṭhaṃ kiṇvāgnikau caiva pibettulyāni pūrvavat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.50"><label>ut.55.50</label> mūtreṇa
                        devadārvagnitriphalābṛhatīḥ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         yavaprasthaṃ phalaiḥ sārdhaṃ kaṇṭakāryā jalāḍhake || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.51"><label>ut.55.51</label> paktvārdhaprasthaśeṣaṃ tu
                        pibeddhiṅgusamanvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         madanālābubījāni pippalīṃ sanidigdhikām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.52"><label>ut.55.52</label> saṃcūrṇya pradhamennāḍyā
                        viśatyetadyathā gudam |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇaṃ nikumbhakampillaśyāmekṣvākvagnikodbhavam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.55.53"><label>ut.55.53</label> kṛtavedhanamāgadhyor lavaṇānāṃ ca
                        sādhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         gavāṃ mūtreṇa tā vartīḥ kārayet tu gudānugāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadyaḥ śarmakarāvetau yogāvamṛtasaṃmatau ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
                        udāvartapratiṣedho nāma (saptadaśo+ādhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcapañcāśattamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ ||55 ||</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.1"><label>ut.56.1</label> athāto visūcikāpratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.8"><label>ut.56.8</label> vātavarconirodhaś ca kukṣau yasya

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.9"><label>ut.56.9</label> duṣṭaṃ tu bhuktaṃ kaphamārutābhyāṃ

                        <caesura/>
                         vilambikāṃ tāṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>bhṛśaduś
                        cikitsyāmācakṣate śāstravidaḥ purāṇāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.10"><label>ut.56.10</label> yatrasthamāmaṃ virujettameva

                        <caesura/>
                         doṣeṇa yenāvatataṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.11"><label>ut.56.11</label> yaḥ śyāvadantauṣṭhanakho

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.12"><label>ut.56.12</label> sādhyāsu pārṣṇyor dahanaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.14"><label>ut.56.14</label>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.15"><label>ut.56.15</label> kṣārāgadaṃ vā lavaṇaṃ viṣaṃ vā

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.16"><label>ut.56.16</label> kaṭutrikaṃ vā lavaṇair upetaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.18"><label>ut.56.18</label> uṣṇābhir adbhir magadhodbhavānāṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.19"><label>ut.56.19</label> chāyāviśuṣkā guṭikāḥ kṛtāstā

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.20"><label>ut.56.20</label> peyādibhir dīpanapācanīyaiḥ
                        samyakkṣudhārtaṃ samupakrameta |

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.21"><label>ut.56.21</label> pravartamānaṃ na yathāsvamenaṃ

                            footnote marker">1</ref>sa śakṛdvamec ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.23"><label>ut.56.23</label> śvāsaś ca pakvāśayaje bhavanti

                        <caesura/>
                         āmodbhave vāntam upakrameta saṃsargabhaktakramadīpanīyaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.24"><label>ut.56.24</label> athetaraṃ yo na śakṛdvamettamāmaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.25"><label>ut.56.25</label> tānyeva vartīrviracedvicūrṇya

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.26"><label>ut.56.26</label> mūtreṣu saṃsādhya yathāvidhānaṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.27"><label>ut.56.27</label> tribhaṇḍiyuktaṃ lavaṇaprakuñcaṃ
                        dattvā viriktakramamācarec ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣveva tailena ca sādhitena prāptaṃ yadi syādanuvāsayec ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.1"><label>ut.57.1</label> athāto 'rocakapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.3"><label>ut.57.3</label> doṣaiḥ pṛthak saha ca
                        cittaviparyayāc ca bhaktāyaneṣu hṛdi cāvatate pragāḍham |
                        <caesura/>
                         nānne rucir bhavati taṃ bhiṣajo vikāraṃ bhaktopaghātamiha pañcavidhaṃ
                        vadanti || | </l>

                    <l/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.4"><label>ut.57.4</label> hṛcchūlapīḍanayutaṃ virasānanatvaṃ
                        vātātmake bhavati liṅgamarocake tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛddāhacoṣabahutā mukhatiktatā ca mūrcchā satṛḍ bhavati pittakṛte tathaiva
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.5"><label>ut.57.5</label> kaṇḍūgutvakaphasaṃsravasādatandrāḥ
                        śleṣmātmake madhuramāsyamarocake tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvātmake pavanapittakaphā bahūni rūpāṇyathāsya hṛdaye samudīrayanti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.6"><label>ut.57.6</label> saṃrāgaśokabhayaviplutacetasastu
                        cintākṛto bhavati so 'śucidarśanāc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāte vacāmbuvamanaṃ kṛtavān pibec ca snehaiḥ surābhir athavoṣṇajalena
                        cūrṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.7"><label>ut.57.7</label>
                        kṛṣṇāviḍaṅgayavabhasmahareṇubhārgīrāsnailahiṅgulavaṇottamanāgarāṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte guḍāmbumadhurairvamanaṃ praśastaṃ snehaḥ
                        sasaindhavasitāmadhusarpiriṣṭaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.8"><label>ut.57.8</label> nimbāmbuvāmitavataḥ kaphaje
                        'nupānaṃ rājadrumāmbu madhunā tu sadīpyakaṃ syāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇaṃ yaduktamathavānilaje tad eva sarvaiś ca sarvakṛtamevam upakrameta || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.9"><label>ut.57.9</label>
                        drākṣāpaṭolaviḍavetrakarīranimbamūrvābhayākṣabadarāmalakendravṛkṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bījaiḥ karañjanṛpavṛkṣabhavaiś ca piṣṭairlehaṃ pacet surabhimūtrayutaṃ
                        yathāvat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.10"><label>ut.57.10</label> mustāṃ vacāṃ trikaṭukaṃ
                        rajanīdvayaṃ ca bhārgīṃ ca kuṣṭhamatha nirdahanīṃ ca piṣṭvā |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtre 'vije dviradamūtrayute pacedvā pāṭhāṃ tugāmativiṣāṃ rajanīṃ ca
                        mukhyām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.11"><label>ut.57.11</label> maṇḍūkimarkamamṛtāṃ ca
                        salāṅgalākhyāṃ mūtre pacet tu mahiṣasya vidhānavidvā |
                        <caesura/>
                         etān na santi caturo lihatas tu lehān gulmāruciśvasanakaṇṭhahṛdāmayāś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.12"><label>ut.57.12</label> sātmyān <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>svadeśaracitān vividhāṃś ca bhakṣyān pānāni
                        mūlaphalaṣāḍavarāgayogān |
                        <caesura/>
                         adyādrasāṃś ca vividhān vividhaiḥ prakārairbhuñjīta cāpi
                        laghurūkṣamanaḥsukhāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.13"><label>ut.57.13</label> āsthāpanaṃ vidhivadatra virecanaṃ
                        ca kuryānmṛdūni śirasaś ca virecanāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         trīṇyūṣaṇāni rajanītriphalāyutāni cūrṇīkṛtāni yavaśūkavimiśritāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.14"><label>ut.57.14</label> kṣaudrāyutāni
                            vitarenmukhabodhanārthamanyāni<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> tiktakaṭukāni ca bheṣajāni |
                        <caesura/>
                         mustādirājataruvargadaśāṅgasiddhaiḥ kvāthairjayenmadhuyutairvividhaiś ca
                        lehaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.15"><label>ut.57.15</label> mūtrāsavairguḍakṛtaiś ca tathā
                        tvariṣṭaiḥ kṣārāsavaiś ca madhumādhavatulyagandhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         syādeṣa eva kaphavātahate vidhiś ca śāntiṃ gate hutabhuji praśamāya tasya
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.16"><label>ut.57.16</label> icchābhighātabhayaśokahate
                        'ntaragnau bhāvān bhavāya vitaret khalu śakyarūpān |
                        <caesura/>
                         artheṣu cāpy apaciteṣu punarbhavāya paurāṇikaiḥ
                            śrutiśatairanumānayettam<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.57.17"><label>ut.57.17</label> dainyaṃ gate manasi bodhanamatra
                        śastaṃ yadyat priyaṃ tadupasevyamarocake tu ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre

                <div n="58" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭāpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.1"><label>ut.58.1</label> athāto
                        mūtrāghātapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.2"><label>ut.58.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.3"><label>ut.58.3</label> vātakuṇḍalikāṣṭhīlā vātabastis
                        tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrātītaḥ sajaṭharo mūtrotsaṅgaḥ kṣayas tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.4"><label>ut.58.4</label> mūtragranthirmūtraśukramuṣṇavātas
                        tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtraukasādau dvau cāpi rogā dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.5"><label>ut.58.5</label> raukṣyādvegavighātādvā
                            vāyurantaramāśirtaḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtraṃ carati saṃgṛhya viguṇaḥ kuṇḍalīkṛtaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.6"><label>ut.58.6</label> sṛjedalpālpamathavā sarujaskaṃ
                        śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātakuṇḍalikāṃ taṃ tu vyādhiṃ vidyāt sudāruṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.7"><label>ut.58.7</label> śakṛnmārgasya basteś ca
                        cāyurantaramāśritaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭhīlāvadghanaṃ granthiṃ karotyacalamunnatam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.8"><label>ut.58.8</label> viṇmūtranilasaṅgaś ca tatrādhmānaṃ
                        ca jāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         vedanā ca parā bastau vātāṣṭhīleti tāṃ viduḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.58.9"><label>ut.58.9</label> vegaṃ vidhārayed yastu
                        mūtrasyākuśalo naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         niruṇaddhi mukhaṃ tasya basterbastigato 'nilaḥ || </l>

                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsitamathaiteṣāmaṣṭānām api vakṣyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.16"><label>ut.59.16</label> aśmarīṃ ca samāśritya yaduktaṃ
                        prasamīkṣya tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathādoṣaṃ prayuñjīta snehādim api ca kramam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.17"><label>ut.59.17</label> śvadaṃṣṭrāśmabhidau kumbhīṃ
                        hapuṣāṃ kaṇṭakārikām |
                        <caesura/>
                         balāṃ śatāvarīṃ rāsnāṃ varuṇaṃ girikarṇikām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.18"><label>ut.59.18</label> tathā vidārigandhādiṃ saṃhṛtya
                        traivṛtaṃ pacet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā tat peyaṃ tena vāpyanuvāsanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.19"><label>ut.59.19</label> dadyāduttarabastiṃ ca
                        vātakṛcchropaśāntaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvadaṃṣṭrāsvarase tailaṃ saguḍakṣīranāgaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.20"><label>ut.59.20</label> paktvā tat pūrvavadyojyaṃ
                        tatrānilarujāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṇotpalādikākolīnyagrodhādigaṇaiḥ kṛtam(śṛtam) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.21"><label>ut.59.21</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ pittakṛcchraṃ
                        nāśayet kṣīram eva vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyāduttarabastiṃ ca pittakṛcchropaśāntaye || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.22"><label>ut.59.22</label> ebhir eva kṛtaḥ snehastrividheṣv
                        api bastiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaṃ virecanaṃ cekṣukṣīradrākṣārasairyutam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.23"><label>ut.59.23</label> surasoṣakamustādau varuṇādau ca
                        yat kṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ tathā yavāgvādi <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>kaphāghāte praśasyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.24"><label>ut.59.24</label> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ kuryād etāneva
                        ca sarvaje |
                        <caesura/>
                         phalguvṛś cīradarbhāśmasāracūrṇaṃ ca vāriṇā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.25"><label>ut.59.25</label> surekṣurasadarbhāmbupītaṃ
                        kṛcchrarujāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathābhighātaje kuryāt sadyovraṇacikitsitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.26"><label>ut.59.26</label> mūtrakṛcchre śakṛjjāte kāryā
                        vātaharī kriyā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedāvagāhāvabhyaṅgabasticūrṇakriyās tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.59.27"><label>ut.59.27</label> ye tvanye tu tathā kṛcchre tayoḥ
                        proktaḥ kriyāvidhiḥ ||</l>
