                         cetasy abhihate puṃsām apasmāro 'bhijāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.6a"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.7"><label>ut.61.7</label> hṛtkampaḥ śūnyatā svedo dhyānaṃ
                        mūrcchā pramūḍhatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nidrānāśaś ca tasmiṃs tu bhaviṣyati bhavanty atha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.8ab"><label>ut.61.8</label> saṃjñāvaheṣu srotaḥsu
                        doṣavyāpteṣu mānavaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.8cd"> rajastamaḥparīteṣu mūḍho bhrāntena cetasā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.9ab"><label>ut.61.9</label> vikṣipan hastapādaṃ ca
                        vijihmabhrūrvilocanaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.9cd"> dantān khādan vaman phenaṃ vivṛtākṣaḥ patet kṣitau || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.10ab"><label>ut.61.10</label> alpakālānataraṃ cāpi punaḥ
                        saṃjñāṃ labheta saḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.10cd"> so 'pasmāra iti proktaḥ sa ca dṛṣṭaś caturvidhaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.11"><label>ut.61.11</label> vātapittakaphairnṝṇāṃ caturthaḥ
                        sannipātataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vepamāno daśan dantān śvasan phenaṃ vamannapi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.12"><label>ut.61.12</label> yo brūyād vikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ
                        māmanudhāvati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato me cittanāśaḥ syāt so 'pasmāro 'nilātmakaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.13ab"><label>ut.61.13</label> tṛṭtāpasvedamūrcchārto
                        dhunvannaṅgāni vihvalaḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.13cd"> yo brūyād vikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ pītaṃ māmanudhāvati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.14"><label>ut.61.14</label> tato me cittanāśaḥ syāt sa
                        pittabhava ucyate |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.14cd"> śītahṛllāsanidrārtaḥ patan bhūmau vaman kapham || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.15"><label>ut.61.15</label> yo brūyād vikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ śuklaṃ
                        māmanudhāvati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato me cittanāśaḥ syāt so 'pasmāraḥ kaphātmakaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.16"><label>ut.61.16</label> hṛdi
                        todastṛḍutkledastriṣvapyeteṣu saṃkhyayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pralāpaḥ kūjanaṃ kleśaḥ pratyekaṃ tu bhavediha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.17"><label>ut.61.17</label> sarvaliṅgasamavāyaḥ
                        sarvadoṣaprakopaje |
                        <caesura/>
                         animittāgamād vyādher gamanād akṛte 'pi ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.18"><label>ut.61.18</label> āgamāccāpy apasmāraṃ vadantyanye
                        na doṣajam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kramopayogād doṣāṇāṃ kṣaṇikatvāt tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.19"><label>ut.61.19</label> āgamād vaiśvarūpyāc ca sa tu
                        nirvarṇyate budhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         deve varṣaty api yathā bhūmau bījāni kānicit || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.20"><label>ut.61.20</label> śaradi pratirohanti tathā
                        vyādhisamudbhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthāyinaḥ kecidalpena kālenābhipravardhitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.21"><label>ut.61.21</label> darśayanti vikārāṃstu
                        viśvarūpānnisargataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         apasmāro mahāvyādhistasmād doṣaja eva tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.22"><label>ut.61.22</label> tasya kāryo vidhiḥ sarvo ya
                        unmādeṣu vakṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         purāṇasarpiṣaḥ pānamabhyaṅgaś caiva pūjitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.23ab"><label>ut.61.23</label> upayogo grahoktānāṃ yogānāṃ tu
                        viśeṣataḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.23cd"> tataḥ sidhyanti te sarve yogair anyaiś ca sādhayet
                        |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.23ef"> śigrukaṭvaṅgakiṇvāhinimbatvagrasasādhitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.24"><label>ut.61.24</label> caturguṇe gavāṃ mūtre
                        tailābhyañjane hitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         godhānakulanāgānāṃ pṛṣatarkṣagavām api || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.25"><label>ut.61.25</label> pitteṣu siddhaṃ tailaṃ ca
                        pānābhyaṅgeṣu pūjitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇair ubhayatobhāgaiḥ śiraś cāpi viśodhayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.26ab"><label>ut.61.26</label> pūjāṃ rudrasya kurvīta
                        tadgaṇānāṃ ca nityaśaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.26cd"> vātikaṃ bastibhiś cāpi paittikaṃ tu virecanaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.27ab"><label>ut.61.27</label> kaphajaṃ
                        vamanairdhīmānapasmāramupācaret |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.27cd"> kulatthayavakolāni śaṇabījaṃ palaṅkaṣām || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.28"><label>ut.61.28</label> jaṭilāṃ pañcamūlyau dve pathyāṃ
                        cotkvāthya yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastamūtrayutaṃ sarpiḥ pacettadvātike hitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.29"><label>ut.61.29</label> kākolyādipratīvāpaṃ siddhaṃ ca
                        prathame gaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         payomadhusitāyuktaṃ ghṛtaṃ tat paittike hitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.30"><label>ut.61.30</label> kākolyādipratīvāpaṃ siddhaṃ ca
                        prathame gaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         payomadhusitāyuktaṃ ghṛtaṃ tat paittike hitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.31"><label>ut.61.31</label>
                        suradrumavacākuṣṭhasiddhārthavyoṣahiṅgubhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhārajanīyugmasamaṅgātriphalāmbudaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.32"><label>ut.61.32</label>
                        karañjabījaśairīṣagirikarṇīhutāśanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ siddhārthakaṃ nāma sarpirmūtracaturguṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.33"><label>ut.61.33</label>
                        kṛmikuṣṭhagaraśvāsabalāsaviṣamajvarān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvabhūtagrahonmādānapasmārāṃś ca nāśayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.34"><label>ut.61.34</label>
                        daśamūlendravṛkṣatvaṅmūrvābhārgīphalatrikaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śampākaśreyasīsaptaparṇāpāmārgaphalgubhiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.35"><label>ut.61.35</label> śṛtaiḥ kalkaiś ca
                        bhūnimbapūtīkavyoṣacitrakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trivṛtpāṭhāniśāyugmasārivādvayapauṣkaraiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.36"><label>ut.61.36</label>
                            kaṭukāyāsadantyugrānīlinīkrimiśatrubhiḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpirebhiś ca gokṣīradadhimūtraśakṛdrasaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.37"><label>ut.61.37</label> sādhitaṃ pañcagavyākhyaṃ
                        sarvāpasmārabhūtanut |
                        <caesura/>
                         cāturthakakṣayaśvāsānunmādāṃś ca niyacchati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.38"><label>ut.61.38</label> bhārgīśṛte pacet kṣīre
                        śālitaṇḍulapāyasam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tryahaṃ śuddhāya taṃ bhoktuṃ varāhāyopakalpayet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.39"><label>ut.61.39</label> jñātvā ca madhurībhūtaṃ taṃ
                        viśasyānnamuddharet |
                        <caesura/>
                         trīn bhāgāṃstasya cūrṇasya kiṇvabhāgena saṃsṛjet || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.40"><label>ut.61.40</label> maṇḍodakārthe deyaś ca
                        bhārgīkvāthaḥ suśītalaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhe kumbhe nidadhyāc ca saṃbhāraṃ taṃ surāṃ tataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.61.41"><label>ut.61.41</label> jātagandhāṃ jātarasāṃ pāyayed
                        āturaṃ bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         sirāṃ vidhyed atha prāptāṃ maṅgalyāni ca dhārayet ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti susrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate bhūtavidyātantre
                        'pasmārapratiṣedho nāma (dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        ||61 ||</p>

                <div n="63" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>triṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.1"><label>ut.63.1</label> athāto rasabhedavikalpamadhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.8"><label>ut.63.8</label> tadyathā madhurāmlaḥ,
                        madhuralavaṇaḥ, madhurakaṭukaḥ, madhuratiktaḥ, madhurakaṣāyaḥ, ete
                        pañcānukrāntā madhureṇa; amlalavaṇaḥ, amlakaṭukaḥ, amlatiktaḥ, amlakaṣāyaḥ,
                        ete catvāro 'nukrāntā amlena; lavaṇakaṭukaḥ, lavaṇatiktaḥ, lavaṇakaṣāyaḥ,
                        ete trayo 'nukāntā lavaṇena; kaṭutiktaḥ, kaṭukaṣāyaḥ, dvāvetāvanukrāntau
                        kaṭukena; tiktakaṣāyaḥ eka evānukrāntastiktena; <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>evam ete pañcadaśa dvikasaṃyogā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                            marker">1</ref> kaṭuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.10"><label>ut.63.10</label> tadyathā madhurāmlalavaṇaḥ,

                        madhuralavaṇakaṭukaḥ, madhuralavaṇātiktaḥ, madhuralavaṇakaṣāyaḥ,
                        madhurakaṭukatiktaḥ, madhurakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, madhuratiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ
                        daśānāṃ trikasaṃyogānāmādau madhuraḥ prayujyate; amlalavaṇakaṭukaḥ,
                        amlalavaṇatiktaḥ, amlalavaṇakaṣāyaḥ, amlakaṭutiktaḥ, amlakaṭukaṣāyaḥ,
                        amlatiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ ṣaṇṇāmādāvamlaḥ prayujyate; lavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ,
                        lavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, lavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ trayāṇāmādau lavaṇaḥ
                        prayujyate; kaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam ekasyādau kaṭukaḥ prayujyate; evam ete
                        trikasaṃyogā viṃśatir vyākhyātāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.11"><label>ut.63.11</label> catuṣkān vakṣyāmaḥ |

                        <caesura/>

                        madhurāmlalavaṇatiktaḥ, madhurāmlalavaṇakaṣāyaḥ, madhurāmlakaṭukatiktaḥ,

                        madhuralavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, madhuralavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ,
                        madhurakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ daśānāmādau madhuraḥ prayujyate;
                        amlalavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ, amlalavaṇakaṭukaṣāyaḥ, amlalavaṇatiktakaṣāyaḥ,
                        amlakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ, evam eṣāṃ caturṇāmādāvamlaḥ; lavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyaḥ,
                        evam ekasyādau lavaṇaḥ; evam ete catuṣkarasasaṃyogāḥ pañcadaśa kīrtitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.13"><label>ut.63.13</label> pañcakān vakṣyāmaḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.14"><label>ut.63.14</label> madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktaḥ,

                        ekasyādāvamlaḥ; evam ete ṣaṭ pañcakasaṃyogā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.63.15"><label>ut.63.15</label> ṣaṭkamekaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ; ekas tu

                        kadācana |

                         ata ūrdhvaṃ dvādaśāśanapravicārān vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        śīroṣṇasnigdharūkṣadravaśuṣkaikakālikadvikālikauṣadhayuktamātrāhīnadoṣapraśamanavṛttyarthāḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.57"><label>ut.64.57</label> tṛṣṇoṣṇamadadāhārtān
                        raktapittaviṣāturān |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchārtān strīṣu ca kṣīṇān śītairannair upācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.58"><label>ut.64.58</label> kaphavātamāmayāviṣṭān viriktān
                        snehapāyinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aklinnakāyāṃś ca narānuṣṇairannair upācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.59"><label>ut.64.59</label> vātikān rūkṣadehāṃś ca
                        vyavāyopahatāṃs tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāyāminaś cāpi narān snigdhairannair upācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.60"><label>ut.64.60</label> medasābhiparītāṃs tu <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>snigdhānmehāturānapi |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphābhipannadehāṃś ca rūkṣairannair upācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.61"><label>ut.64.61</label> śuṣkadehān pipāsārtān durbalānapi
                        ca dravaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         praklinnakāyān vraṇinaḥ śuṣkairmehina eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.62"><label>ut.64.62</label> ekakālaṃ bhaveddeyo
                        durbalāgnivivṛddhaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         samāgnaye tathāhāro dvikālam api<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >1</ref> pūjitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.63"><label>ut.64.63</label> auṣadhadveṣiṇe deyas
                        tathauṣadhasamāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mandāgnaye rogiṇe ca mātrāhīnaḥ praśasyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.64"><label>ut.64.64</label> yathartudattastv āhāro
                        doṣapraśamanaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ataḥ paraṃ tu svasthānāṃ vṛttyarthaṃ sarva eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pravicārānimānevaṃ dvādaśātra prayojayet<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.65"><label>ut.64.65</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ daśauṣadhakālān
                        vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrābhaktaṃ prāgbhaktam adhobhaktaṃ madhyebhaktamantarābhaktaṃ sabhaktaṃ
                        sāmudgaṃ muhurmuhur grāsaṃ grāsāntaraṃ ceti daśauṣadhakālāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.66"><label>ut.64.66</label> tatrābhaktaṃ tu yat kevalam
                        evauṣadham upayujyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.67"><label>ut.64.67</label> vīryādhikaṃ bhavati bheṣajam
                        annahīnaṃ hanyāt tathā<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>++āmayamasaṃśayamāśu caiva |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>tad bālavṛddhavanitāmṛdavas
                        tu pītvā glāniṃ parāṃ samupayānti balakṣayaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.68"><label>ut.64.68</label> prāgbhaktaṃ nāma yat
                        prāgbhaktasyopayujyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.69"><label>ut.64.69</label> śīghraṃ vipākam upayāti balaṃ na
                        hiṃsyād annāvṛtaṃ na ca muhur vardanān nireti |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāgbhaktasevitam athauṣadham etad eva dadyāc ca
                        vṛddhaśiśubhīrukṛśāṅganābhyaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.70"><label>ut.64.70</label> adhobhaktaṃ nāma <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>yadadho bhaktasyeti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.71"><label>ut.64.71</label> madhye bhaktaṃ nāma yan madhye
                        bhaktasya pīyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.72"><label>ut.64.72</label> pītaṃ yad annam upayujya tad
                        ūrdhvakāye hanyād gadān bahuvidhāṃś ca balaṃ dadāti |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhye tu pītam apahanty avisāribhāvād ye madhyadeham abhibhūya bhavanti
                        rogāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.73"><label>ut.64.73</label> antarābhaktaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>nāma yad antarā pīyate
                        pūrvāparayor bhaktayoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.74"><label>ut.64.74</label> sabhaktaṃ <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>nāma yat saha bhaktena || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.75"><label>ut.64.75</label> pathyaṃ sabhaktam abalābalayor hi
                        nityaṃ tad dveṣiṇām api tathā śiśuvṛddhayoś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdyaṃ manobalakaraṃ tvatha dīpanaṃ ca pathyaṃ sadā bhavati
                        cāntarabhaktakaṃ yat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.76"><label>ut.64.76</label> sāmudgaṃ <ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref>nāma yad bhaktasyādāvante ca pīyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.77"><label>ut.64.77</label> doṣe dvidhā pravisṛte tu
                        samudgasaṃjñam ādyantayor yad aśanasya niṣevyate tu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.78"><label>ut.64.78</label> muhur muhur nāma sabhaktam
                        abhaktaṃ vā yad auṣadhaṃ muhur muhur upayujyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.79"><label>ut.64.79</label> śvāse muhurmuhuratiprasṛte ca
                        kāse hikkāvamīṣu sa vadantyupayojyametat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.80"><label>ut.64.80</label> grāsaṃ tu yatpiṇḍavyāmiśram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.81"><label>ut.64.81</label> grāsāntaraṃ<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> tu yadgrāsāntareṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.82"><label>ut.64.82</label> grāseṣu<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> cūrṇam abalāgniṣu dīpanīyaṃ vājīkarāṇy api tu
                        yojayituṃ yateta |
                        <caesura/>
                         grāsāntareṣu vitared vamanīyadhūmān śvāsādiṣu prathitadṛṣṭaguṇāṃś ca lehān
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.83"><label>ut.64.83</label> evam ete daśauṣadhakālāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.64.84"><label>ut.64.84</label> visṛṣṭe viṇmūtre viśadakaraṇe
                        dehe ca sulaghau |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśuddhe codgāre hṛdi suvimale vāte ca sarati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathānnaśraddhāyāṃ klamaparigame kukṣau ca śithile |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradeyastv āhāro bhavati bhiṣajāṃ kālaḥ sa tu mataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.1"><label>ut.65.1</label> athātas tantrayuktim adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.2"><label>ut.65.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.3"><label>ut.65.3</label> dvātriṃśattatantrayuktayo bhavanti
                        śāstre |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadyathā adhikaraṇaṃ, yogaḥ, padārthaḥ, hetvarthaḥ, uddeśaḥ, nirdeśaḥ,
                        upadeśaḥ, apadeśaḥ, pradeśaḥ, atideśaḥ, apavarjaḥ, vākyaśeṣaḥ, arthāpattiḥ,
                        viparyayaḥ, prasaṅgaḥ, ekāntaḥ, anekāntaḥ, pūrvapakṣaḥ, nirṇayaḥ, anumataṃ,
                        vidhānam, anāgatāvekṣaṇam, atikrāntāvekṣaṇaṃ, saṃśayaḥ, vyākhyānaṃ,
                        svasaṃjñā, nirvacanaṃ, nidarśanaṃ, niyogaḥ, vikalpaḥ, samuc cayaḥ, ūhyam,
                        iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.4"><label>ut.65.4</label> atrāsāṃ tantrayuktīnāṃ kiṃ
                        prayojanam ucyate vākyayojanam arthayojanaṃ ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.5"><label>ut.65.5</label> bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ
                        asadvādiprayuktānāṃ vākyānāṃ pratiṣedhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         svavākyasiddhir api ca kriyate tantrayuktitaḥ<ref rend="superscript
                            footnote marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.6"><label>ut.65.6</label> vyāktā noktās tu ye hy arthā līnā
                        ye cāpy anirmalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         leśoktā ye ca kecit syus teṣāṃ cāpi prasādhanam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.7"><label>ut.65.7</label> yathāmbujavanasyārkaḥ pradīpo
                        veśmano yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         prabodhasya prakāśārthaṃ tathā tantrasya yuktayaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.8"><label>ut.65.8</label> tatra yam artham adhikṛtyocyate tad
                        adhikaraṇaṃ; yathā rasaṃ doṣaṃ vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.9"><label>ut.65.9</label> yena vākyaṃ yujyate sa yogaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā tailaṃ pibec cāmṛtavallinimbahiṃsrābhayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge |
                        <caesura/>
                         ityatra tailaṃ siddhaṃ pibediti prathamaṃ vaktavye tṛtīyapāde siddhamiti
                        prayuktaṃ, evaṃ dūrasthānām api padānāmekīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.10"><label>ut.65.10</label> yo 'rtho 'bhihitaḥ sūtre pade vā
                        sa padārthaḥ; padasya padayoḥ padānāṃ vārthaḥ padārthaḥ; aparimitāś ca
                        padārthāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā snehasvedāñjaneṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu dvayostrayāṇāṃ vārthānām upapattir
                        dṛśyate, tatra yo 'rthaḥ pūrvāparayogasiddho bhavati sa grahītavyaḥ; yathā
                        devotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ity ukte sandihyate buddhiḥ katamasya <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>vedasyotpattiṃ vakṣyatīti,
                        yataḥ ṛgvedādayas tu vedāḥ; vida vicāraṇe, vidḷ lābhe, ity etayoś ca
                        dhātvoranekārthayoḥ prayogāt,tatra pūrvāparayogam upalabhya pratipattir
                        bhavati āyurvedotpattim ayaṃ vivakṣur iti; eṣa padārthaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.11"><label>ut.65.11</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>yad anyad uktam
                        anyārthasādhakaṃ bhavati sa hetvarthaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā mṛtpiṇḍo 'dbhiḥ praklidyate tathā māṣadugdhaprabhṛtibhir vraṇaḥ
                        praklidyata iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.12"><label>ut.65.12</label> samāsavacanam uddeśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā śalyam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.13"><label>ut.65.13</label> vistaravacanaṃ nirdeśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā śārīram āgantukaṃ ceti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.14"><label>ut.65.14</label> evamityupadeśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā tathā na jāgṛyād rātrau divāsvapnaṃ ca varjayet iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.15"><label>ut.65.15</label> anena kāraṇenety apadeśaḥ,
                        yathāpadiśyate madhuraḥ śleṣmāṇam abhivardhayatīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.16"><label>ut.65.16</label> prakṛtasyātikrāntena sādhanaṃ
                        pradeśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā devadattasyānena śalyam uddhṛtaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref>tathā yajñadattasyāpy ayam uddhariṣyatīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.17"><label>ut.65.17</label> prakṛtasyānāgatasya sāghanam
                        atideśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā yato 'sya vāyur ūrdhvam uttiṣṭhate tenodāvartī syād iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.18"><label>ut.65.18</label> abhivyāpyāpakarṣaṇamapavargaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā asvedyā viṣopasṛṣṭāḥ, anyatra kīṭaviṣāditi || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.19"><label>ut.65.19</label> yena padenānuktena vākyaṃ
                        samāpyeta sa vākyaśeṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā śiraḥpāṇipādapārśvapṛṣṭhodarorasāmityukte puruṣagrahaṇaṃ vināpi
                        gamyate puruṣasyeti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.20"><label>ut.65.20</label> yadakīrtitamarthādāpadyate
                        sārthāpattiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā odanaṃ bhokṣye ity ukte 'rthādāpannaṃ bhavati nāyaṃ pipāsur yavāgūm
                        iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.21"><label>ut.65.21</label> yadyatrābhihitaṃ tasya
                        prātilomyaṃ viparyayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā kṛśālpaprāṇabhīravo duś cikitsyā ityukte viparītaṃ gṛhyate dṛḍhādayaḥ
                        sucikitsyā iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.22"><label>ut.65.22</label> prakaraṇāntareṇa <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>samāpanaṃ prasaṅgaḥ, yadvā
                        prakaraṇāntarito yo 'rtho+<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>asakṛduktaḥ samāpyate sa prasaṅgaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣastasmin kriyā so 'dhiṣṭhānamiti
                        vedotpattāvabhidhāya, bhūtacintāyāṃ punaruktaṃ yato 'bhihitaṃ
                        pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa iti, sa khalveṣa karmapuruṣaś
                        cikitsādhikṛta iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.23"><label>ut.65.23</label> (<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref>sarvatra) yad avadhāraṇenocyate sa ekāntaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā trivṛd virecayati, madanaphalaṃ vāmayati (eva) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.24"><label>ut.65.24</label> kvacit tathā kvacid anyatheti yaḥ
                        so 'nekāntaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā kecid ācāryā bruvate dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ, kecid rasaṃ, kecid vīryaṃ
                        kecid vipākam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.25"><label>ut.65.25</label> ākṣepapūrvakaḥ praśnaḥ
                        pūrvapakṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā kathaṃ vātanimittāś catvāraḥ pramehā asādhyā bhavantīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.26"><label>ut.65.26</label> tasyottaraṃ nirṇayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā śarīraṃ prapīḍya paś cād adho gatvā vasāmedomajjānuviddhaṃ mūtraṃ
                        visṛjati vātaḥ, evam asādhyā vātajā iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.27"><label>ut.65.27</label> tathā coktam kṛtsnaṃ śarīraṃ
                        niṣpīḍya medomajjāvasāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhaḥ prakupyate vāyustenāsādhyās tu vātajāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.28"><label>ut.65.28</label> paramatamapratiṣiddham anumatam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā anyo brūyāt sapta rasā iti, taccāpratiṣedhād anumanyate kathaṃcid iti
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.29"><label>ut.65.29</label> prakaraṇānupūrvyābhihitaṃ
                        vidhānam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā sakthimarmāṇyekādaśa prakaraṇānupūrvyābhihitāni || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.30"><label>ut.65.30</label> evaṃ vakṣyatītyanāgatāvekṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ślokasthāne brūyāt cikitsiteṣu vakṣyāmīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.31"><label>ut.65.31</label> yatpūrvamuktaṃ
                        tadatikrāntāvekṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā cikitsiteṣu brūyāt ślokasthāne yadīritam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.32"><label>ut.65.32</label> ubhayahetudarśanaṃ saṃśayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā talahṛdayābhighātaḥ prāṇaharaḥ, pāṇipādacchedanamaprāṇaharam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.33"><label>ut.65.33</label> tantre 'tiśayopavarṇanaṃ
                        vyākhyānam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā iha pañcaviṃśatikaḥ puruṣo vyākhyāyate, anyeṣvāyurvedatantreṣu
                        bhūtādiprabhṛtyārabhya <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>cintā
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.34"><label>ut.65.34</label> anyaśāstrāsāmānyā svasaṃjñā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā mithunam iti madhusarpiṣorgrahaṇaṃ; lokaprasiddhamudāharaṇaṃ <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.35"><label>ut.65.35</label> niś citaṃ vacanaṃ nirvacanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā āyurvidyate 'sminnanena vā āyurvindatītyāyurvedaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.36"><label>ut.65.36</label>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>dṛṣṭāntavyaktir nidarśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā agnir vāyunā sahitaḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>kakṣe vṛddhiṃ gacchati tathā vātapittakaphaduṣṭo vraṇa iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.37"><label>ut.65.37</label> idam eva kartavyam iti niyogaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā pathyam eva bhoktavyam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.38"><label>ut.65.38</label> idaṃ cedaṃ ceti samuc cayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā māṃsavarge eṇahariṇādayo lāvatittiriśāraṅgāś ca pradhānānīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.39"><label>ut.65.39</label> idaṃ vedaṃ ceti vikalpaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā rasaudanaḥ saghṛtā yavāgūrvā (bhavatviti) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.40"><label>ut.65.40</label> yadanirdiṣṭaṃ buddhyā<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>+avagamyate tadūhyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā abhihitam annapānavidhau caturvidhaṃ cānnam upadiśyate bhakṣyaṃ
                        bhojyaṃ lehyaṃ peyamiti, evaṃ caturvidhe vaktavye dvividham abhihitam; idam
                        atrohyam annapāne viśiṣṭayor dvayor grahaṇe kṛte caturṇām api grahaṇaṃ
                        bhavatīti; caturvidhaś cāhāraḥ praviralaḥ, prāyeṇa dvividha eva; ato dvitvaṃ
                        prasiddham iti |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcānyat annena bhakṣyam avaruddhaṃ, ghanasādharmyāt; peyena lehyaṃ,
                        dravasādhamyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.41"><label>ut.65.41</label> bhavanti cātra <ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref>sāmānyadarśanenāsāṃ vyavasthā
                        saṃpradarśitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣas tu yathāyogam upadhāryo vipaś citā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.42"><label>ut.65.42</label> dvātriṃśadyuktayo hy etās
                        tantrasāragaveṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         mayā samyag vinihitāḥ śabdārthanyāyasaṃyutāḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
                            marker">1</ref> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.43"><label>ut.65.43</label> yo hy etā vidhivad vetti
                        dīpībhūtās tu buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa pūjārho bhiṣakśreṣṭha iti dhanvantarer matam ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre tantrabhūṣaṇādhyāyeṣu
                        tantrayuktir nāma (tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||65
                        ||</p>
                </div>
                <div n="66" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.1"><label>ut.66.1</label> athāto doṣabhedavikalpamadhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.2"><label>ut.66.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.3"><label>ut.66.3</label> aṣṭāṅgavedividvāṃsaṃ divodāsaṃ
                        mahaujasam |
                        <caesura/>
                         chinnaśāstrārthasaṃdehaṃ sūkṣmāgādhāgamodadhim | </l>

                    <l/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.4"><label>ut.66.4</label> viśvāmitrasutaḥ śrīmān suśrutaḥ
                        paripṛcchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣaṣṭirdoṣabhedā ye purastātparikīrtitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.5"><label>ut.66.5</label> kati tatraikaśo jñeyā dviśo vāpy
                        athavā triśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā saṃśayacchinmahātapāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.6"><label>ut.66.6</label> prītātmā nṛpaśārdūlaḥ<ref
                            rend="superscript footnote marker">1</ref> suśrutāyāha tattvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayo doṣā dhātavaś ca purīṣaṃ mūtram eva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.7"><label>ut.66.7</label> dehaṃ sandhārayanty ete hy
                        avyāpannā rasair hitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣaḥ ṣoḍaśakalaḥ prāṇāś caikādaśaiva ye || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.8"><label>ut.66.8</label> rogāṇāṃ tu sahasraṃ yac chataṃ
                        viṃśatir eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         śataṃ ca pañca dravyāṇāṃ trisaptatyadhikottaram || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.9"><label>ut.66.9</label> vyāsataḥ kīrtitaṃ taddhi bhinnā
                        doṣāstrayo guṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviṣaṣṭidhā bhavanty ete bhūyiṣṭham iti niś cayaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.10"><label>ut.66.10</label> traya eva pṛthak doṣā dviśo nava
                        samādhikaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trayodaśādhikaikadvisamam adhyolbaṇais triśaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.11"><label>ut.66.11</label> pañcāśadevaṃ tu saha bhavanti
                        kṣayamāgataiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                        >1</ref>kṣīṇamadhyādhikakṣīṇakṣīṇavṛddhais tathāparaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.12"><label>ut.66.12</label> dvādaśaivaṃ samākhyātāstrayo doṣā
                        dviṣaṣṭidhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         miśrā dhātumalairdoṣā yānty asaṃkhyeyatāṃ punaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.13"><label>ut.66.13</label> tasmāt prasaṅgaṃ saṃyamya
                        doṣabhedavikalpanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogaṃ viditvopacared rasabhedair yathair itaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.14"><label>ut.66.14</label> bhiṣak kartātha karaṇaṃ rasā
                        doṣās tu kāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāryam ārogyam evaikam anārogyam ato 'nyathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.15"><label>ut.66.15</label> adhyāyānāṃ tu ṣaṭṣaṣṭyā
                        grathitārthapadakramam |
                        <caesura/>
                         evam etad aśeṣeṇa tantram uttaram ṛddhimat || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.16"><label>ut.66.16</label> spaṣṭagūḍhārthavijñānam agāḍham
                        andacetasām |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāvidhi yathāpraśnaṃ bhavatāṃ parikīrtitam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.66.17"><label>ut.66.17</label> sahottaraṃ tv etad adhītya sarvaṃ
                        brāhmaṃ vidhānena yathoditena |
                        <caesura/>
                         na hīyate 'rthān manaso 'bhyupetād etad vaco brahmam atīvasatyam ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantre doṣabhedavikalpo nāma
                        ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||66 ||</p>
                </div>
                <div>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti sauśrute āyurvedaśāstre uttarasthānaṃ samāptam || </p>

                </div>


            </div>
        </body>
